Spanish Lerroux Cabinet Resigns; Due to President's Approval of Amnesty Bill; Deemed a Vote of No Confidence in the Government 70

Madrid. The Lerroux Radical Cabinet resigned en masse at noon today because it did not approve of President Zamara's political amnesty bill. Disturbances have occurred throughout the country in recent days. General strikes and semi-revolutionary political unrest have occurred in Madrid, San Sebastian, and other major cities. Political observers say that the cabinet's mass resignation may lead to a serious government crisis. Premier Lerroux declared after submitting his resignation that his cabinet had decided to oppose the president's amnesty bill because the cabinet clearly no longer had the president's trust. The amnesty bill included General Chappuis, who had committed serious treason and was sentenced to death, but the sentence was later commuted to life imprisonment. After accepting the resignation, the President immediately convened a meeting of leaders of various political parties to seek new figures to form a cabinet. (25th National Telegram)

Spain and Peru Approve Silver Agreement; Now Reaching Implementation Stage 71

(Washington) U.S. Under Secretary of State Phillips announced today that all silver agreements in the London Conference have now reached the implementation stage because Spain and Peru have formally ratified the agreement. (24th National Telegram)

Reasons for the Fall in Silver Prices (London) London financiers believe that the fall in silver prices is due to the failure of the silver faction in the United States because President Roosevelt refused to adopt their proposals. Financiers also believe that, given the current world situation, the normal price of silver should be around 18.5 to 19 pence. China is the most important factor in the silver market. China has recently kept silver prices about one penny below parity, so the sale by the United States will bring silver prices in line with Chinese prices. The London silver market was stable after the listing of silver prices today. (Reuters Telegram)

Speculators' Efforts Fall Short (New York) Foreign speculators intended to use a surprise attack to cause the U.S. dollar to fall, but today this plan has completely failed. Since last Friday, their manipulation plan has begun to be active, and the value of the dollar has gradually fallen. Foreign speculators all thought that success was at hand, but unexpectedly, on Saturday morning, the Ministry of Finance suddenly issued a notice stating that the U.S. government had decided to maintain the gold price so that it would match the dollar's price, resulting in failure. (24th National Telegram)

Roosevelt Does Not Want to Make New Experiments; Silver Legislation Hopeless; Ministry of Finance Releases List of Silver Depositors; Silver Sold Off, Market Price Plunges 72

(Washington) President Roosevelt does not seem to be eager to engage in new experiments on monetary issues. Originally, the president had great hopes for the policy of buying gold abroad and devaluing the dollar, but judging from his recent declarations, it can be said that he has expressed disappointment. Since this policy has not had the expected effect on gold, it does not seem that it will be effective on silver either. Some observers point out that President Roosevelt is now skeptical of the new theories of Professor Warren of London (who proposed buying gold). Warren's name is no longer mentioned, and the President's attitude towards monetary and price-raising issues is now very conservative, probably for this reason. (25th Havas Telegram)

(Washington) Although the silver faction in Congress is enthusiastic and taking the offensive, the 25 members of the Senate Presiding Officers, led by Laboring, today compiled the Senate agenda for the future and removed the silver issue. The Senate's current agenda is that Congress will [adjourn?] at the end of June. [Unclear] President Roosevelt, [Congress?] must extend the session by early June. (24th Havas Telegram) (Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau today sent the Senate a list of silver depositors in the country, mostly large companies and banks, such as Manhattan Bank with 11 million ounces of silver, Chase National Bank with 4 million ounces, and certain prominent individuals also on the list. (24th Havas Telegram)

(Washington) After the Ministry of Finance released the list of silver depositors in the country this afternoon, large quantities of silver were sold off in the market, causing silver prices to plummet. Regarding the release of the list, the financial community believes that it is not surprising that the list includes many large banks and silver brokerage firms, because these companies all have important business relationships with the Far East. Although they sometimes engage in speculative behavior, the government does not need to accuse them of speculation. Currently, some in the Senate are beginning to advocate for an investigation into silver speculation. (24th Havas Telegram)

London Disarmament Talks: Britain and Italy Moving Towards Common Goal; Scale of Disarmament May Be Lowered to Achieve Success; Germany Still Insists on Principle of Equality in Armaments 73

(London) Recent events have made a disarmament treaty with an outline of British proposals all the more necessary. This was the conclusion of the talks in London between Italian representative Suvich, British Foreign Secretary Simon, and Eden. The Italian government believes that if the entire British plan cannot be accepted by others, it may be better to lower the scale and make a smaller disarmament in order to achieve success. The British side believes that the British plan has reduced difficulties compared to the original disarmament proposals because: (1) Some countries with a genuine spirit of self-restraint have reduced their armaments to a lower standard than they can permanently agree to, such as the British Air Force and the French Army; (2) If the purpose is to limit armaments according to the current level, it is still doubtful whether some countries will allow people to investigate their armaments and numbers; (3) A static agreement will necessarily involve restrictions on the number of various armaments, and it will be difficult to implement supervised management of this aspect. It is expected that when the current talks end tomorrow, there will be tangible progress towards a common goal.

German Special Envoy Explains Mission 74

Ribbentrop, the German special representative for discussing disarmament issues, told Reuters in Berlin today that his task was to pave the way for a disarmament treaty. This treaty, based on equality, could give Europe peace and restore the necessary sense of security and trust for the recovery of European economic life. The right to self-defense and equality cannot be denied to Germany. No one can deny the moderation of Germany's demands for national defense tools. Hitler's appropriate armaments demands have shown an unshakable determination to defend the country and mark the beginning of a new era of genuine peace in Europe. (24th Reuters Telegram)

French Foreign Minister Successfully Lobbies Poland; French and Polish Interests are Shared; Alliance Has Not Wavered 75

Bardoux Leaves Warsaw for Czechoslovakia, Relations Between Poland and Czechia Expected to Improve. Krakow, Poland. (25th Havas Agency Telegram)

Warsaw. French Foreign Minister Bardoux has completed his official visit to Poland. The government issued a communiqué reporting the results of Bardoux's trip, stating that the first thing to declare is that the 1921 French-Polish alliance treaty remains the basis of relations between the two countries. Regarding the disarmament issue, Bardoux explained France's views in detail, which seem to be in line with Poland's views. In addition, Poland intends to maintain a good-neighborly policy with its neighbors and intends to negotiate with Soviet Russia to extend the effective period of the mutual non-aggression treaty between the two countries (Soviet Russia and Poland are in negotiations, see our telegram of April 21). As for the Czech arrest and subsequent release of Polish people, it is hoped that it can be resolved peacefully. French Foreign Minister Bardoux also discussed economic issues and prepared to hold negotiations in Warsaw to establish a temporary solution. (24th Havas Agency Telegram) (Paris) Local newspapers believe that French Foreign Minister Bardoux's talks with Polish General Pilsudski in Warsaw are the most important event of Bardoux's trip. The Daily News reported that Pilsudski had repeatedly stated that the French-Polish agreement was unchangeable and told Bardoux that Poland would continue to support the League of Nations as the only mechanism for resolving international problems. According to reports, Pilsudski's friendship with Soviet Russia is limited to the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty and will not form a closer relationship. Furthermore, he did not mention the dispute between Poland and Czechia, which France values, which is strange. Regarding the German-Polish treaty, he discussed it in detail, but stated that there are no secret agreements between Germany and Poland. Regarding Germany's restoration of armaments, he reportedly held an extremely positive observation point and sarcastically suggested to Bardoux that France would eventually be oppressed and should improve its current attitude towards Germany. Furthermore, because Polish Foreign Minister Beck will accompany Bardoux to Krakow today, it is believed that Bardoux's trip to Warsaw seems to be a victory on the surface. (24th National Agency Telegram)

丨April 25th, Reuters Special Commodity Report丨 Gold and Silver 77

London Gold: The London gold price today was 135 shillings and 6.5 pence, a decrease of 4.5 pence compared to yesterday's price.

London Silver: The London silver market was weak today, with spot prices at 18 pence 75 and futures at 18 pence 875, both down 5625. This was mainly due to selling by the United States and China, as well as weak buying interest. The New York silver market opened weakly today due to unfavorable foreign news and the liquidation of long positions. The opening drop was quite sharp, about 1.5 US cents lower than London, which triggered buying. About half of these transactions came from London. The market gradually stabilized before noon, and prices recovered slightly because the liquidations after the opening had been absorbed. However, according to Washington news, the silver faction seems to be failing, so the market is not very calm. Therefore, the opening price of the forward silver market here today was reduced by 55 to 100 pounds compared to yesterday's closing price.

Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market was weak at 5:30 PM today. The spot price was 52 rupees and 8 annas, down 1 rupee and 5 annas. Futures both fell, one by 1 rupee and 4 annas, and the other by 1 rupee and 5 annas.

Exchange Rates 78

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market this morning, European operators repurchased US dollars, causing the British-American exchange rate to open down 125 to 5 dollars and 1 dime and 5 cents. Before noon, prices gradually trended down to 5 dollars, 1 dime, 4 cents, and 4375, a decrease of 5625 compared to the opening. Also, one US dollar equals 3 shillings and 10 pence and 5629 British gold.

British-French: The opening was 77 francs 37, the same as yesterday's closing price. Later, there were mixed ups and downs. At 3 PM, the price was 77 francs 53. US-British: The New York exchange rate for British pounds opened at 5.14.125 today, a sudden drop of 1 cent compared to the previous day. The second round recovered slightly, changing to 5.14.625. The third, fourth, and fifth rounds also fell slightly to 5.14.25. The sixth round was the lowest at 5.14.00.

US-French: The New York exchange rate for French francs opened at 6.64.00 today, a decrease of .2.

Cotton and Wheat 79

American Cotton: When the cotton market opened today, prices rose due to improvements in the actual position, large-scale purchases by peers, the capture of short positions, and reactive purchases, as well as purchases by European and Japanese merchants. The liquidation of long positions and selling from the local South and New Orleans were all absorbed. After the opening, news from Liverpool turned positive, and peers bought in droves, but foreign merchants sold due to the spread of May futures settlements and the weakness of the US dollar, which slightly offset the rise. The New York market issued 20,200 bales of May delivery notices, while New Orleans issued 33,100 bales.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market opened weaker this morning. At 1 PM, the price for July futures was 5.79, down 6 pounds.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was closed today.

Securities 81

In New York today, security opening prices showed narrow and mixed fluctuations. Japanese Troops Encircle the Anti-Japanese Volunteers in Hulin丨Chen Dongshan and Gao Yushan Defend丨丨 98

A correspondent in Harbin reports that the Anti-Japanese Volunteers in eastern Jilin Province were active near Suifenhe last month, occupying Hulin and besieging Mishan. The units of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers led by Chen Dongshan and Gao Yushan are echoing the units of Wang Delin and Kong Xianwu in the Tokyo Cheng area, forming a connection. The Hirose unit of the 10th Division of the Japanese Army stationed in Harbin attacked with a large force. At that time, the Chen and Gao units were being pursued by the Japanese troops in Fujin from the rear, facing enemies on both sides for a time. They retreated to Guliyulin in Hulin, where they defended the dangerous terrain and gradually replenished their forces, waiting for another opportunity. The 10th Division of the Japanese Army still sent the Kaneko branch of the Takamori unit stationed at Maqiaohe along Mishan Hulin, to attack in coordination with the 4th Cavalry Brigade of the puppet Jilin Army, led by Guo Baoshan. The Fujimoto detachment of the Osedo unit of the Japanese Army stationed in Yanshou connected with the 7th Brigade of the puppet Jilin Army, led by Bai Wenqing, and went straight to Hulin. The Yoshizawa detachment of the Japanese Army stationed in Duojin went to Baoqing, attacking the flank of Hulin. After the fierce battle last month, the Chen and Gao units of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers suffered heavy casualties and were short of ammunition. Because the city defenses of Hulin offered no protection, they joined more than a thousand Anti-Japanese Volunteers of Wang Sanhao in Raohe at Guliyulin, using each other as a stronghold. The Japanese army's attack plan seems to be to encircle them on three sides. If the mountains are difficult to break through, they also plan to besiege the Anti-Japanese Volunteers for a long time. Therefore, all roads leading out of Guliyulin have been fortified with blockhouses by the Japanese army, which are equipped with machine guns to monitor the Anti-Japanese Volunteers. Each blockhouse is stationed with 100 to 150 Japanese soldiers. The original name of the valley was Dumugou. The area is about 80 li from east to west and about 160 li from north to south.

The main products are opium, timber, and fur. It is a large forest area. The logged forests and empty land are scattered with more than a thousand households. The roads leading out of the valley include the four main roads of Mishan, Tuanshanzi, Baoqing, and Hulin. Among them, the road between Mishan and Hulin is relatively flat, and cars can be driven in winter. Today, all four main roads have been blocked by the Japanese army. The grain stored in Guliyulin can be eaten for six months. Currently, Gao Yushan and Chen Yushan have sent troops to occupy the traffic crossings based on the natural barriers, digging trenches for long-term defense. On the one hand, they led the troops to implement a per capita land allocation system, separately reclaiming land as a self-sufficiency measure. Therefore, it currently forms a standoff with the Japanese army. This unit of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers is the most organized and strongest among the various units in Jilin and Heilongjiang, so the Japanese and puppet troops are eager to eliminate it. Chen and Gao are also afraid of being besieged for a long time and running out of food, so they sent representatives to Suifenhe, Yimianpo, Muling, Ning'an, Dongning, Dunhua and other places to contact various branches of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers, intending to use the strategy of "besieging Wei to rescue Zhao" to lift the siege of Guliyulin. Recently, Genshan, Jinshan, Qingshan, and Daqingshan in the mountains of Yimianpo and other places, and famous mountains in the Weihuling area, Delin, Chaoyang, Xishuangsheng and other branches of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers are several thousand strong, and are active around Hengdaohezi, aiming to capture Suifenhe to force the Japanese army to rescue. Therefore, in the past week, the Dongtie Hasui Line has become tense again, which is caused by the activities of the Anti-Japanese Volunteers. (18th)

Bandit Liu Completely Annihilated, All Armies are Searching for Remnants 99

Jinan correspondent reports that when Liu Guitang's remaining bandits were fleeing westward at Henggou at 3:00 AM on the 23rd, they were intercepted by Kang Zhankui's regiment, killing dozens. They then broke up into smaller groups and fled separately. A larger group desperately fled along the border between Rizhao and Juxian. Finally, they fled west along the Xun River from Liangshankou in Rizhao and were intercepted by various armies, putting them in a very embarrassing situation. They passed Zhuzhou Nanling, entered Juxian County, passed Tianzhuang, Mazhuang, Yaobu, Heijian, and fled into the mountains, hiding in the wheat fields around Xianglushan Langwoshan Maqiyao. The bandits also changed into white trousers and jackets and, because they had been fleeing day and night in Shandong for a month, had no time to shave. On the evening of the 23rd, they busily shaved their hair with knives, preparing to hide with guns. On the morning of the 24th, two central airplanes flew in the direction of reconnaissance, but because the bandits were scattered and hiding, they were not discovered. Later, the bandits traveled south from the disordered mountains, passing Shanghu, Jishan Xipi, and Tangzhuang. At about 10:00 AM, they arrived near Tubaiyanggou and Xiabaiyanggou and were detected by the bandit suppression army. Zhan Shutang, commander of the 81st Division, led a battalion of infantry and a company of cavalry to attack Baiyanggou from Liugou to the northwest. Liu's battalion of the 22nd Division also advanced from Dadian via Laozi Lve to the southeast. The bandits suddenly encountered Zhan's unit and, not daring to resist, fled in a panic to Dongjiantou. At that time, Liu's battalion also arrived to intercept and suppress them. The bandits turned back south and passed Shangxiabaiyanggou to Sanguanmiao Wanghailou. Zhan and Liu's units immediately surrounded and attacked them from both sides. The bandits could not break through despite fighting to the death. By 4:00 PM, the situation was completely resolved. In this battle, more than 60 rifles, 4 pistols, more than 60 bandits were killed, and more than 30 were captured. More than 70 good horses were obtained. No one escaped. Liu's battalion returned to Juxian, and Zhan Shutang is searching for the remaining bandits in Sanguanmiao near Shangxiabaiyanggou. Another small group, about twenty people, fled into Rizhao on the 23rd, from Hujiazhuang to the north of Sanzhuang. The Rizhao People's League immediately surrounded them. The bandits did not resist and claimed to be willing to surrender their guns. The district chief asked County Chief Yang Jinbiao for instructions. On the afternoon of the 24th, they completed the surrender of their weapons. One battalion of Gao Lantian's unit is now stationed in San Zhuang for suppression. Liu's bandits had been raiding Shandong for nearly 40 days, and now they have been completely resolved, removing a major threat from North China. Now the bandit suppression armies are following Han Fuju's orders, searching for the remaining bandits and returning to defense. Ma Guanyi's brigade will soon arrive in Zaozhuang, board trains and return to Dezhou. Gao Lantian's regiment will also go to Gaomi and return to its original defense in Haiyang. Kang Zhankui's regiment arrived in Qingzhou on the 24th, boarded trains and came west. Tang Bangzhi's brigade will return to Jinan. Also, when the bandits passed Rizhao, the Lian Zhuang Hui captured two or thirty scattered bandits. When the bandits fled in Shichang, Ma Guanyi's brigade also captured more than a dozen people in the north. According to reports, the 22nd Division seized a large amount of military equipment from the bandits this time, including six light machine guns and more than two hundred rifles. Other parts have not yet been counted and reported. (24th)

Lu Han Dispels Resignation Intentions, Jiang Bocheng Arrives in Jinan to Console and Retain 100

Jinan correspondent reports that Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuju had asked to resign because Liu's bandits had been raiding Shandong for more than a month before the bandits were mostly suppressed. However, the past command and arrangements were very troublesome, so he was physically unwell. Furthermore, because Liu's bandits were such a small group and could not be immediately eliminated in Shandong for more than a month, he felt that he had not fulfilled his military duties. Therefore, he recently telegraphed National Government Chairman Lin Sen, Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, and Military Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, requesting to resign from all his positions so that he could recuperate. After the telegrams were sent, the central government believed that North China was in a time of crisis and relied heavily on him. How could it allow him to withdraw? Lin, Wang, and Chiang all sent telegrams of consolation and encouragement. Chiang even telegraphed Han again, saying that at this time of national crisis, the security of North China is of great importance to the overall situation, urging him to do his best and eliminate the intention to resign. He also ordered Chiang Po-cheng to come to Jinan from Peiping to personally convey his condolences and retain him. Chiang Po-cheng arrived in Jinan from Peiping on the morning of the 22nd and personally spoke with Han about everything. After being persuaded by various parties, Han replied to Chairman Chiang this evening, saying that he would comply and cancel his resignation, and would temporarily be responsible for Shandong's military and political affairs as usual, and would strive to serve the public despite his illness.

Also, news reports that Shen Honglie, Ge Guangting, Jiang Bocheng and others came to Jinan some days ago to persuade and retain Han Fuju, who had resigned from the central government. Han has now dispelled his intention to resign after being persuaded by various parties, and has been meeting and talking with Jiang, Shen and Ge for days. Today (24th) at 10:00 AM, Han, accompanied by Jiang, Shen and Ge, took a car to Luokou to visit the Yellow River and had lunch together in Luokou. Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun, Finance Director Wang Xiangrong, Education Director He Siyuan, Construction Director Zhang Honglie, Provincial Government Committee Member Zhang Cheng and others also went along. They returned to Jinan at 2:00 PM. Jiang Bocheng, with Han having dispelled his intention to resign and his mission completed, was originally scheduled to leave Jinan and return to Peiping tonight (24th). Ge Guangting and Shen Honglie also planned to return to Qingdao, but were retained by Han and changed their plans to leave Jinan separately tomorrow morning (25th). The following is a record of Jiang Bocheng's conversation: [Chairman Han's reason for resigning this time was actually because of his eagerness to seek improvement

and to govern well. Chairman Chiang saw Chairman Han as the pillar of North China and relied heavily on him, so he telegraphed to earnestly retain him. After I arrived in Jinan, I worked with Mayor Shen (Honglie), Chairman Ge (Guangting) and local gentry and merchants to do our best to retain him. Chairman Han has dispelled his intention to resign and will continue to be responsible for Shandong's military and political affairs. Regarding the Shandong party affairs disputes, Chairman Chen (Lifu) originally planned to come to Shandong for a trip to convene various committee members to talk and explain everything, but because of his busy public affairs, he will not come north for the time being. After I came to Jinan, I invited Chairman Zhang (村) and Chairman Li (Wenzhai) and others to talk. The misunderstandings between the two sides have been resolved, and the party affairs work will continue as usual, without any problems. As for the Jinan Arsenal, Chairman Han believes that it is expensive and difficult to operate, and plans to ask the Central Government to take it over. After I met with Chairman Han and discussed it, it was decided to ask the Central Government to take over, and I have telegraphed Chairman Chiang to report this situation, asking him to instruct the Ministry of Military Administration to send personnel to take over. I have completed my public affairs in Jinan, so I will return to Peiping immediately.] etc. (24th)

Public Appeal by Songjiang Citizens Regarding River Dredging 101

Tang Gengyang and other citizens of Songjiang collectively sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters, the Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman, the Director of Finance Chen, and the Director of Construction Shen, regarding river dredging. The telegram stated: All previous river dredging projects in Songjiang were planned and carried out based on the convenience of weather, geography, and manpower, always achieving results with minimal cost. Now, the County Magistrate Jin Tigan and the technical director Xu Mo Jia, for the sake of dredging the city river, are colluding with local powerful merchants and cleverly imposing harsh taxes. During the busy farming season of the plum rains, they recklessly recruit hundreds of strong out-of-town laborers, squandering more than three times the provincial funds and people's wealth, causing great harm to the local area. We respectfully present this to your esteemed office: (1) After the Qingming Festival, farming activities are in full swing. At this time, to cut off the dam and the water source deprives the rice paddies of irrigation. This is the first thing that hinders agricultural work. (2) In the late spring climate, there is continuous overcast and rain. Dredging the river by pumping water causes it to overflow as quickly as it's pumped. Squandering funds and wasting time will only lead to clumsiness. This is the second thing that violates the seasons. (3) The dredging cost of our Songjiang city river has never exceeded 20,000 yuan. Taking the two instances of the 6th and 14th years of the Republic as examples, the cost of earth excavation, regardless of difficult labor and transportation, averaged only 55 cents. The total dredging cost was less than 20,000 yuan. The established case can be reviewed. However, this time, there is intentional delay, and recruitment and bidding are only conducted when the farming season is approaching. As a result, the Taichang Gravel Company, which has no river dredging experience, rises to take the contract. Consequently, the price of 20,000 yuan in previous years suddenly jumps to a huge sum of 63,000 yuan. (According to the county government's announcement, in addition to the construction fee of 28,000 yuan approved by the provincial departments, the designated local donation portion requires 35,000 yuan.) This is the third thing that falsely squanders provincial and local funds. (4) The labor cost per cubic foot in Songjiang has suddenly increased, nominally at 40 cents, but in reality, difficult labor and long-distance transportation are secretly added, making it as high as 1.84 yuan per cubic foot. In reality, there is no so-called difficult or long-distance transportation in dredging the city river. This is how they deceive superiors, defraud the public, and cleverly embezzle funds. This is the fourth thing that is unacceptable. (5) Songjiang is located in a vital area of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, often infested with bandits. Now, in a place where farming is flourishing, all industries are withering, and vagrants are abundant, suddenly recruiting thousands of strong out-of-town laborers and gathering them in an important city will inevitably disrupt the local area. Recently, the initial dredging in Huayang Town, east of the city, has already caused neighboring residents to suffer from the indiscriminate dumping of river mud, leading to frequent disputes. With such disturbances at the beginning, the future is long and the risks are even more worrying. This is the fifth thing that is unacceptable. (6) Songjiang is a water town, and waterway transportation is crucial to the prosperity of commerce. In recent years, Songjiang's commerce has declined, and the city is in recession, far less prosperous than Qingpu's Zhujiajiao town. The reason is that the rivers are not smooth, causing congestion. River dredging should be a priority, but it is not done from the source, and only the surface mud is dug in the center of the city river, which is practically the same as not dredging at all. This is the sixth thing that is unacceptable. (7) There should be a budget for river dredging, but the budget has never been published. There should be a scheduled date for the contractor to be paid, but the payment date has not been announced. Not only is the public completely unaware of this important matter, but even the standing committee members of the river dredging project are in a fog, unable to inquire. This is the seventh thing that is unacceptable. (8) At the beginning of the preparations, the county government proposed that all river dredging staff should be paid salaries. The upright gentlemen of Songjiang, unwilling to fill their own pockets with the people's hard-earned money, requested the cancellation. However, the county government's existing public officials who are assigned to river dredging duties all hold concurrent positions and receive concurrent salaries. The people pay taxes to support these public officials with regular monthly salaries, and when their duties arise and are related to construction, these natural committee members want to obtain this undeserved benefit. This is the eighth thing that is unacceptable. In addition to these eight unacceptable things, there is also the matter of soliciting donations, which goes against public opinion. Ordinary people are distinguished as gentry and wealthy, and certain types of businesses are selected and tasked with paying special donations. Songyi is located in the interior, and most people live by digging wells and farming, content with their daily lives, so there are no wealthy merchants to speak of, and even fewer wealthy gentry to behold. Imposing donations here is already the height of exploitation. Furthermore, there is a rental housing donation, where each household must donate two months' rent, half from the landlord and half from the tenant, assuming that those who rent houses from others must have surplus funds, and those who live under someone else's roof can spare one month. Who knows that families of eight have no other income and rely on this for their livelihoods? Donating these two months' rent would starve their eight mouths, and those who live under someone else's roof suffer even more. Moreover, during the January 28th Shanghai Incident, there was a proposal to collect two months' rent, entrusting the police chief to supervise with inspectors and hiring employees from the Chamber of Commerce to collect donations from house to house. The people of Songjiang scraped together what they could to provide it. To this day, there has not been a single report of the expenses, shown to the public. All of the above are facts, and violating the three major principles of weather, geography, and manpower is especially unreasonable. We have no choice but to request your esteemed office to swiftly order the cessation of forced donations, and to send personnel to thoroughly investigate the truth of the construction funds, to punish corruption and bring peace to the good people. The people of Songjiang would be fortunate, and the local area would be fortunate. Citizens of Songjiang County, Tang Zhigao, Sun Huzhan, Lu Guiliang, Wu Cunfu, Xia Xiasan, Song Yunsheng, Wang Zhongwei, and Liang Ruoyuan, respectfully kowtow.

Songjiang: Investigation of the Lantern Festival Incident Nears 102

The Provincial Government ordered the county to thoroughly investigate the incident in Tinglin Township, Punan, where villagers destroyed the Public Security Bureau during a lantern festival. The county police authorities have strictly arrested and interrogated the villagers involved. Details have been reported in the Shanghai and Songjiang newspapers. It is now learned that Xu Weisheng and others, natives of Songjiang residing in Beijing, after seeing reports on the cause of the incident, which included the tearing of the national flag and the burning of the Premier's portrait by members of the Public Security Bureau, believe that there is a need to present the case to the province for thorough investigation. They have specifically attached newspapers and telegraphed the provincial government, requesting the dispatch of personnel to thoroughly investigate and deal with the matter. The county government has now received a directive from the provincial government ordering a thorough investigation and response.

Recent Developments in Land Survey and Measurement 103

Our county previously received an order from the province to carry out land survey and measurement. During the tenure of former County Magistrate Shen, funds were raised for the land survey and measurement, and a Land Survey and Measurement Fund Management Committee was established, with funds deposited in the Farmers Bank. Personnel were also dispatched to make preparations. The Provincial Land Bureau also sent personnel to Songjiang last year to measure the central point and establish a marker in the eastern city, which was carried out quite intensively. Measurement has already begun in the Xijiaoziyu area of the fifth Ku of the tenth district at the beginning of this month. At the same time, the measured fields are being drawn into maps. The aforementioned work team members were sent by the Provincial Land Bureau, with He Xuzu, leader of the first group of the Provincial Land Survey and Measurement team, leading the team to Songjiang. An office was set up in Qiujiawan, and 50 surveyors were recruited to serve. After the measurement of the tenth district is completed, the first district will be measured in sequence. It is now learned that the Provincial Land Bureau has sent five employees, including Yan Zheng, to Songjiang yesterday to carry out measurements at the marker site in the East Gate. Group leader He has sent a letter to the chief of the first district to request assistance. After the land survey and measurement in our county is completed in the future, registration will be carried out, which requires personnel with considerable knowledge to serve. Therefore, County Magistrate Jin has selected Hu Runlin and Shen Shuyong to go to the province for training, and they have already set off.

Commencement of Work by Party Affairs Commissioner 104

In order to promote the development of social undertakings in various counties, the Provincial Party Headquarters has divided all counties in the province into several districts, sending commissioners to provide guidance, stationed in the central county to set up offices. Our county and neighboring counties are listed as the second district, with our county as the central county. Niu Changyao, a member of the Provincial Party Committee, serves as the guidance commissioner, and the office is organized within the First District Party Headquarters in the city. Work has begun today. County Magistrate Jin and the county executive committee visited him together. It is heard that Commissioner Niu will actively promote cooperative undertakings in our county to benefit the rural areas.

Suzhou: Reaction to the Reception of County-Owned Telephone Services 105

The Jiangsu Construction Department intends to take over the county's city and township long-distance telephone services in order to unify telephone management. The County Chamber of Commerce specifically submitted a petition to the Provincial Government yesterday (24th), stating that the telephones in all townships of the county were constructed with donations from the local people, costing 60,000 to 70,000 yuan. They are purely part of the county's public property and are also a type of county-run enterprise. If the takeover is approved, not only will local construction lack guarantees, but who would be willing to try to run public enterprises? Please instruct the Construction Department to exempt the takeover. Even if it concerns unified telephone administration and the request is not adopted, it is requested that a fair valuation be made and the compensation be paid to value the county's assets and respect public opinion.

Wuxi: Construction of Changqiao Bridge on the Five-Li Lake Has Commenced 106

The County Construction Bureau technicians have completed the measurement of the road surface of the Huanhu Road on the Five-Li Lake in the western township of our county. The entire line is 11 kilometers and 89 meters long, and it has been determined that a Changqiao Bridge should be built at Baojiekou, with the foundation at Baojieqinshan, passing near Huiquanshan. The head of the third district, Yu Xunzhen, and the bridge construction director, Rong Desheng, have negotiated and agreed. Because this matter is significant and the construction period is very long, it has been presented to the county government for approval and a notice has been issued to inform the people on both sides of the river to cooperate in order to facilitate the progress. Subsequently, Rong Desheng ordered the construction of more than 20 factory buildings at the base of the bridge on both the east and west sides, and contracted the project to Gu. Cement, steel, yellow sand, and foreign pine and other application materials were transported to the site, and central wooden piles were nailed in the center of the river as a standard for work. After breaking ground at the end of last month, construction has commenced. First, wooden piles are nailed and erected at the bridge abutments on both ends, and foreign pine planks are laid on top as the initial work for making cement piles. There are dozens of workers actively working, and there are two ferries traveling back and forth between the two ends. The bridge project is very large, with an estimated 60 loops and a grand scale, requiring more than 100,000 yuan, which can be called the largest project in the county.

Changzhou: County Government Welcomes the Capture of Notorious Bandit Gu Yuliang 107

The notorious bandit Gu Yuliang of Wu County, using the alias Jiang Helin, previously lived in Gujia Village in the third district. He was fierce and engaged in robbery, murder, arson, and all kinds of evil. He was able to fire a box gun with both hands. For example, he robbed the house of Wang Songyun, the township assistant of Qianlou Luan Township, and set fire to dozens of houses, robbed boats at the wharf, and killed and wounded many people. Some of his accomplices were arrested and executed, but Gu Yuliang pretended to die of illness and went into hiding in Shanghai. Every winter, he would return to his hometown with accomplices to rob. Recently, in February, he privately carried a box gun and a rifle in the vicinity of Baima Temple in Jintan County to rob. The rifle failed to fire continuously and was surrounded and captured by the public, and sent to the county for sentencing to fifteen years' imprisonment. When County Magistrate Cai of our county heard the news, he first sent a letter to the county government to inquire, and then received a reply stating that he had committed many crimes in Changzhou and was allowed to be extradited. Yesterday (24th), he prepared a document and sent police to Jintan to escort the bandit Gu Yuliang to Changzhou for interrogation.

Zhenjiang: Chairman Chen Rectifies Discipline 108

Provincial Chairman Chen pays great attention to the discipline of his subordinates. According to reports, public officials in this city's entertainment venues often rely on their credentials to enter without buying tickets. Considering this related to the business of various entertainment venues, a notice was issued today instructing all departments, bureaus, and the garrison headquarters to strictly order their subordinates not to engage in the aforementioned behavior again, and informed the Security Office and the Municipal Public Security Bureau to conduct strict inspections and arrest offenders at any time.

Ningbo: Resignation of Yin County Magistrate Chen Baolin 109

Chen Baolin, the county magistrate of Yin County, has been in office for more than five years since taking office in the 18th year of the Republic. Recently, due to the difficulty of various measures, he submitted his resignation to the Civil Affairs Department when he visited the province a few days ago. Yesterday, he sent a letter instructing the county government secretariat and the first and second sections to expedite the transfer matters. The Yin County Cultural and Historical Committee has sent a telegram to the province yesterday to request him to stay.

The Sheng Kang Qianzhuang Robbery Case Solved 110

After the Sheng Kang Qianzhuang on Cuiya Street in this city was robbed at 2:00 pm on the 31st of last month, Zhao Shunfa, the head of the detective team of the Security Division, immediately purchased a wide range of informants and cooperated in the investigation. It was later found that the case was committed by Yu Aliang, who lives in a certain village west of Yinjiang Bridge in Yinxi. Yu is a well-known bandit with many accomplices, who has been kidnapping and robbing in Shanghai. In March of this year, he committed a crime in Shanghai. Due to the urgent pursuit by the police, it was difficult to settle down. He and two gangs of bandits came to Ningbo with weapons to rob the Sheng Kang Qianzhuang. After obtaining the loot, they fled to their hometown to hide. On the 2nd of this month, they went to Shanghai, and on the 21st, they took the Hongxing wheel to Ningbo again. Captain Zhao received a telegram from Shanghai and waited at the port in advance. As soon as the wheel arrived at the port, he arrested the bandit Yu, took him back to the team for interrogation.

Local News

Philippine Speaker Quezon Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday; Various Chinese and Foreign Groups Warmly Received Him One After Another; Quezon and Others Returned to the Philippines by the Original Vessel at Six O'Clock This Morning 111

Philippine Senate Speaker Quezon, accompanied by his wife and several Philippine senators, went to the United States to discuss the issue of independence. Now that they have achieved success, they arrived in Shanghai on the Empress of Canada. The Pan-Pacific Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Mayor Wu all held banquets to entertain them one after another. They are scheduled to return to the Philippines by the original vessel this morning. The details are as follows:

Special Ship to Greet 112

The ship entered port at around 8 o'clock yesterday morning and docked at the Qichangzhan wharf in Pudong at 9:45. The welcoming personnel included Tang Shixuan, representative of Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Zhao Tiezhang, section chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai office, and personnel from the U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai. A Jinghui small vessel of the Jianghai Customs was specially prepared to greet them in advance. After Mr. Quezon exchanged greetings with each of the welcoming personnel on the ship, he transferred to the special ship at 9:30 and sailed back to the Xinguang wharf, where he went ashore and went to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to rest.

Accompanying Personnel 113

Those who came with Mr. Quezon, in addition to his wife and one son and two daughters, included Senator Quireno and his wife and daughter, Ernan and his wife and daughter, Capelton, Nieto, and Las and his wife and daughter, Mrs. Maria Picameiro, Mrs. Dulores Picameiro, Ms. Homolo, Mrs. Lama, Mrs. Achangyu, Mr. Losen Shore, Dr. Cabenuno, Mr. Jasu, Mr. Keyuan, Mr. Quireno, Mr. Pield, Ms. Carmen, Mr. Gaxia, and Mr. Anke, a total of more than 30 people.

Joint Association Banquet 114

At 12:30 yesterday afternoon, the Pan-Pacific Association held a special banquet at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund. Many members from various Chinese and foreign circles attended. The former Minister of Foreign Affairs, Wang Zhengting, presided over the meeting and delivered a welcome speech. Mr. Quezon delivered a reply on behalf of the group. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until about 2 o'clock in the afternoon.

Photo of Philippine Speaker Quezon (X) Passing Through Shanghai (Taken by Wang Kai)

Chamber of Commerce Reception 115

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce held a tea party in the conference room on the third floor of the chamber at 5:00 pm yesterday because Mr. Quezon had negotiated several times for the Philippine independence movement and has now achieved satisfactory results. The Philippines is a region where overseas Chinese gather, and overseas Chinese merchants occupy a dominant position. In the future, after the Philippines becomes independent, trade between China and the Philippines will inevitably flourish. In addition to Quezon and his wife and the entire delegation, those present included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of Public Utilities Xu Peihuang, Municipal Government Secretary Tang Shixuan, Municipal Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Committee Members Wang Yansong, Pei Yunqing, Chen Zheqing, Yu Zuoting, Wen Lanting, and chairmen of various trade associations, Chen Liting and his wife, Liu Wang Liming, and others, totaling more than 80 people. Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting and Xie Fusheng served as the translator.

Chairman's Speech 116

Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered a welcome speech, saying, "On October 12, 1929, ten groups gathered here to welcome you. At that time, there was a saying: 'Mr. Quezon is a leader who seeks happiness for the Philippines, with great aspirations and diligent achievements.' All of us present here deeply admire him.

We hope to continue to work hard year after year and achieve a Chinese idiom, which is 'Where there is a will, there is a way.' We said this sentence exactly four and a half years ago. Mr. Quezon has surprisingly returned to his hometown with his successful mission to report to his compatriots. This is such a fortunate thing. We believe that the Philippines' position is the vanguard of peace in the Pacific, and the success of the Philippines in the political aspect is of great significance to the future of the Pacific. Therefore, our small tribute today can also be called a celebration banquet for Mr. Quezon. The communication between the Chinese and Filipino peoples is earlier than the communication with Europeans and can be called old friends. The communication has been long, and for hundreds of years, the two peoples have had a history of intermarriage, so they can also be called close neighbors with kinship. Because we have these two qualifications, our country is willing to cite a Chinese idiom, which is 'Nothing is too good to talk about.' Today, we will contribute this meaning to Mr. Quezon. The Filipino people are the most capable of absorbing new ideas, without being rigid or stubborn, and are the fastest progressing people. We know that the reform of the Philippines' internal affairs, the popularization of education, and the development of the economy have only been in history for four or fifty years, but in terms of its achievements, it can be at least equivalent to the progress of a century. Therefore, based on the past history, we can make predictions for the future. We believe that the next ten years will be a time for the Filipino people to struggle harder. We believe that the result of the Filipino people's efforts can build an Eastern Switzerland and an Eastern Belgium in the Pacific. This is a prediction we dare to make. As old friends, and as close neighbors with kinship, we plan to organize a commercial delegation to visit your country in the autumn and winter to observe the progress of various facilities recently, so as to learn from our country and seek the development of commerce between us, so that the connection between the two peoples will become closer and closer. I hope Mr. Quezon will be willing to convey this idea in advance. With the return trip imminent, I would like to raise a glass to celebrate Mr. Quezon and the success of the Filipino people's efforts, and wish them unlimited progress in the future."

Quezon's Reply 117

Quezon replied, "The Philippine Independence Movement delegation, on its way back from the United States, when passing through Shanghai, is grateful for this grand celebration meeting held by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and commercial groups. I respectfully express my gratitude on behalf of the entire delegation. Recalling four years ago, when I passed through Shanghai for the Philippine independence movement, the Chamber of Commerce and others welcomed me, and at that time, there was a saying that 'the Philippine independence will eventually be successful.' At that time, it was still a kind of hope and prediction, but now it has become a reality. The result of this trip to the United States is that from next year, the entire island will be completely autonomous, and all officials will be appointed by Filipinos, but the American flag will still be hung. After ten years, the American flag can be removed and become a new country in the Pacific recognized by the world. The people of our country are very happy with the success of this trip by the delegation. The ideal of the past has now become a brilliant reality. I am one of the most enthusiastic about the independence movement. In my childhood, I had the idea of the independence of the Philippines in my mind, and since I grew up, I have taken the independence of the Philippines as my only mission. Today, I am deeply ashamed that the Chairman gave a speech to celebrate the success and development of the independence of the Philippines. At the same time, I sincerely accept this kindness. The relationship between China and the Philippines has a long history. The Philippines has been in communication with China since the beginning of its founding. I hope that friendship will increase and commerce will prosper in the future. The blood relationship between the people of the two countries is especially valuable. Almost all famous people in the Philippines have Chinese blood, and the large number of overseas Chinese in the Philippines, their high moral character, and their purity and credibility are especially welcomed by Filipinos. The chairman said that there will be a commercial investigation team to the Philippines this autumn, which is deeply welcomed. If you say sightseeing, I dare not accept it. If you want to seek mutual understanding and practical cooperation between the two countries, you must have frequent contact. A year ago, a semi-official investigation team from the Philippines came to China and was well received. The Chinese delegation will be greatly welcomed this autumn. I also have a request to the chairman: I hope to pull Mayor Wu to go together, which will be even more welcome. The enthusiasm of the Philippines in welcoming the Chinese delegation must far exceed that of any other visiting groups or representatives, and I hope that this will be the first time for the Chinese investigation team to go to the Philippines, and there will be countless trips back and forth, so that the commercial and national feelings of the two countries will increase day by day. Because the interests of the two countries are related, China's progress is the Philippines' progress, and the Philippines' progress is China's progress. I am honored that the chairman celebrated and praised the future of our delegation. I respectfully transfer it to China. China is gradually progressing today. Because of its vast land and abundant resources, and its excellent people, it will surely be the leader of the world in the future."

Leaving Shanghai That Evening 118

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng and his wife held a banquet at Wanglu on Haig Road at 8:00 last night to wash away the fatigue for Mr. Quezon. In addition to Mr. Quezon and many Philippine senators, dignitaries from various Chinese and foreign circles in this city were also invited to accompany them. After the banquet, Mr. Quezon and the senators who came with him, as well as the welcoming personnel from the Philippines to Shanghai, and Secretary Niagawa, boarded the Empress of Canada and left Shanghai at around 6:00 this morning to return to the Philippines.

Japanese Envoy Returned to His Country Yesterday Morning; Will Return to Shanghai in Three Weeks 119

Japanese Ambassador to China Arimiyoshi Akira, accompanied by his wife, Counselor Yamada, Secretary Yokokawa, and others, left Shanghai by Japanese ship Shanghai Maru at 9:00 yesterday morning to return to his country. Arimiyoshi drove to the Huishan Wharf from Bishun Road at 8:30. The counselor of the Japanese Embassy, Arimoto, and personnel from the Consulate General were all present to see him off. It is also learned that after Arimiyoshi arrives in Japan, he will immediately meet the Japanese Emperor to report on various situations in China, and will stay for three weeks before returning to Shanghai.

It was originally scheduled for Counselor Honno to return to his country with the Japanese envoy yesterday morning, but he was prevented from doing so due to an incident and rescheduled his departure for next week.

Australian Deputy Prime Minister Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning; Accompanied by Six Advisors, Secretaries, and Reporters; Will Go to Beijing on the 28th and Cross to Japan on the 7th 120

Australian Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Foreign Affairs Lanshan, accompanied by a group of seven advisors, etc., came to investigate the political and economic situation in the Far East. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning by French mail ship Datnan from Hong Kong. Mayor Wu invited them to a banquet tonight, scheduled to go to Beijing on the 28th to visit our country's authorities, and then go north to Ping, and cross to Japan from Shanghai on the 7th of next month. The details are as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 121

The French ship Datnan, on which Mr. Lan was traveling, entered the Songkou yesterday morning and berthed at the China Merchants Bureau Zhongzhan Wharf on the outer Hongqiao at 7:00. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng's representative, Secretary Geng Jiaji, and Yu Ming, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, went to the wharf to welcome him. He rested on the ship and went ashore at about 9:00 before going to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund with his secretary to rest.

Accompanying Personnel 122

In addition to Advisor Lao Aibo, those who arrived in Shanghai on the same ship as Mr. Lan yesterday morning included Mr. Lan's private secretary Stanley Xidi, Assistant Secretary Ferguson, and four officials from the Australian Intelligence Department, including Mr. Moore. In addition, there were two journalists who came with Mr. Lan: Kato Lake, the Australian journalist representative, and Murray, the reporter from the Shan Heerde Telegraph Agency. As for Mr. Lan's wife and daughter, they are scheduled to come to Shanghai from Java on May 6.

Itinerary 123

After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Lan attended the Anvik General Assembly's dance party at the Ritz Hotel at 9:30 last night. This morning, he will first visit British Commercial Counselor Biel, and then visit the banking community. In the evening, he will attend a banquet hosted by Mayor Wu Tiecheng. On the 27th, he will attend a banquet hosted by the British Consul General at the consulate at noon. On the 28th, after attending a banquet hosted by the British Chamber of Commerce at noon, he will take a train to Beijing that evening. After arriving in Beijing on the morning of the 29th, Mr. Lan will first visit the British Consul General in Beijing and our government officials, and introduce and meet with Wang Jian, the Minister of Foreign Affairs. He will also visit the famous scenic spots in the capital. In the evening, he will attend a banquet hosted by the Beijing Municipal Government. On the morning of May 1, he will leave Beijing by train and arrive in Ping on the morning of the 2nd.

He will first visit British Ambassador Gadgan and then go sightseeing. On the 4th, he will return south from Ping. On the 6th, he will return to Shanghai. On the morning of the 7th, he will take the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru to Japan and transfer to Tokyo from Yokohama. Mr. Lan is scheduled to stay in China for only 12 days.

Mr. Lan's Interview 124

Mr. Lan is currently about fifty-six or fifty-seven years old. He is a graduate of the University of Melbourne in Australia. He has held important positions in the Australian government, including Minister of Interior, Minister of Industry, and Minister of Foreign Affairs. This time, he has come to investigate the Dutch East Indies, Singapore, Saigon, Hong Kong, and other places. According to Mr. Lan's interview with reporters, his first visit to the Dutch East Indies was because that location is closest to Australia, so he went there first. In the future, the Australian side may add commercial commissioners in important commercial ports in the Far East, but this is not an urgent need. Mr. Moore, an intelligence officer who came with me this time, is preparing to handle the liaison work needed for commerce, he said.

More than a Thousand Representatives of the Zhabei District Rent Reduction Association Petition 125

Student representatives explained their plight, and Section Chief Hong promised to forward it. The Zhabei District General Association of the Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, based on the resolution of the representatives' conference the day before yesterday, gathered at its Baoshan Road clubhouse at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. More than 1,000 representatives from various branch associations arrived, each holding a white flag with slogans such as "[Reduce Rent to Revitalize the Zhabei Market]", "[Rent Reduction as the Vanguard for the Prosperity of the Zhabei Market]", "[Request the Mayor to Consider the Citizens Surviving After the War]", and "[Demand the Mayor to Quickly Reduce Rent]". Under the command of Ma Rugen, Jiang Yanqing, Feng Qibiao, and others, they boarded more than 30 freight trucks and proceeded in an orderly manner towards the municipal government. The citizens on Baoshan Road and Jiangwan Road applauded and cheered on both sides, almost emptying the streets. Unexpectedly, while passing the West Road of the Sports Association, the Public Security Bureau of the Fifth Precinct of the Fifth District received an order from the municipal government to stop their progress. Therefore, the bureau specially dispatched all armed police to stop them. After repeated negotiations by the responsible personnel of the association, the bureau chief requested instructions from the municipal government. The municipal government agreed to send representatives to the bureau to meet face-to-face. A temporary citizens' representatives' conference was immediately held on that road, and Sun Junman, Xu Zaikang, Wei Zhiqiu, Lü Chunsan, Zhang Jimao, and five other representatives were publicly elected to go to the municipal government with a small number of people to request the mayor to alleviate the suffering of the citizens of Zhabei after the disaster and to provide relief for the current situation. Because the mayor had other important business that day, Section Chief Hong of the Second Department was specially appointed to receive them on his behalf. The representatives of the association presented the suffering of the people in Zhabei who had been affected by the disaster, as well as the various oppressions they suffered from landlords, coupled with the decline of commerce and the sluggish market, and all the phenomena. They even asked Section Chief Hong to forward the suffering of the citizens of Zhabei to the mayor. Section Chief Hong was responsible for replying, promising to fully convey it to the mayor. At the same time, Section Chief Hong stated that he would make all the facilities in Zhabei after the war benefit all the citizens of Zhabei. The representatives of the association were satisfied, bid farewell, and led the representatives of the entire district back to the Baoshan Road clubhouse, reported the situation of the petition to the municipal government to the branch associations. All the representatives were satisfied and decided to hold another representatives' conference of various branch associations the next day.
