Special Feature

Tong Xingbai Speaks: The Knowing and Doing Problem of the New Life Movement 222

(1) Chen Dongbai's Notes: The Modern Thought Society recently held its third academic lecture in the auditorium of the Provincial Shanghai Middle School, inviting Mr. Tong Xingbai, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, to speak on the topic of "The Knowing and Doing Problem of the New Life Movement." The following is a transcript of his speech:

Chairman, fellow students, today I am very happy to be invited by the Modern Thought Society to come here to give a lecture and to meet and talk with you. Today I am talking about [The Problem of Knowing and Doing in the New Life Movement]. This problem seems too abstract and difficult to explain, because [knowing] and [doing] seem to involve philosophical problems. Today, let's combine the knowing and doing problem with the New Life Movement to study it. After studying it, we can know how to do the New Life Movement. If we find a correct path, we will not be at a loss and confused. This is very meaningful for promoting the New Life Movement. I will now explain it to you in several points.

First, the historical explanation of the New Life Movement: Many people say that the New Life is the opposite of the old life, and the New Life is opposed to the old life. The New Life is good, so the old life must be bad. But according to my research, this is not the case, because the New Life wants to restore propriety, justice, integrity, and shame, and propriety, justice, integrity, and shame have flourished for a long time in Chinese history, so the old life is not necessarily bad. Therefore, I advocate that it should be divided into three names, one is the [New Life] that we are currently talking about, one is the [Old Life] in Chinese history, and the other is the [Bad Life] that has developed in the last hundred years. The reason for advocating the New Life is to correct the bad life, and to create a New Life, we must find its advantages in all the lifestyles in history for reference. Therefore, these three kinds of life, the New Life, are in line with the current era and our living environment. The Old Life, although it has its advantages, has too many formalities and is not in line with modern life. Talking about the New Life as a standard, the Old Life is too much, and the Bad Life is not enough. Too much or not enough is not in line with our lives.

Page 15

Shen Bao Guohuo Weekly

Contribution Speech

In Memory of Mr. Xiang Songmao 223

— Yang An

It has been more than two years since Mr. Xiang Songmao disappeared. Based on the evidence from various sources, there is no doubt that Mr. Xiang was murdered. The cruel and vicious hands of the enemy cause everyone to feel heartbroken and indignant. Moreover, society's loss of a kind, amiable, and enthusiastic supporter of domestic goods, Mr. Xiang, has especially dealt a major blow and sacrifice to the domestic goods industry. I still remember five or six years ago when the reporter wrote an article in the Machine Union Journal titled [How Capable is Mr. Songmao, Recovering 3.6 Million Yuan in Rights Each Year], and more than two or three hundred people wrote letters wanting to meet Mr. Xiang and visit his Guben Soap Factory. Because before Yinben soap, the soaps we used every day were all foreign soaps. Mr. Xiang, with his perseverance and ambition, took over the factory run by the Germans and managed it himself, enduring all kinds of hardships and difficulties to achieve today's success. He was also able to produce new drugs to replace imported medicines. How could such achievements not inspire admiration and respect? Therefore, Mr. Xiang's actions deserve to be called the perfect person in the domestic goods industry. In the history of domestic goods, he can be immortal for thousands of years. I hope that comrades in the domestic goods industry will continue Mr. Xiang's unfinished business with Mr. Xiang's perseverance and spirit.

Highly Important Regulations Regarding Country of Origin Labeling 224

— Yang An

Recently, the Jianghai Customs issued a notice stating: "[The implementation of the 'Regulations Regarding Country of Origin Labeling for Imported Goods' has been postponed to July 1st of this year, as announced on November 22nd of last year. Now, according to government orders, the implementation of the 'Regulations Regarding Country of Origin Labeling for Imported Goods' should be further postponed, and further instructions will be issued once a specific date is set.]"

Upon reading this notice, one cannot help but feel apprehensive. Whose obstruction is causing this repeated postponement, and whose intention is it? The only lifeline for protecting domestic goods relies on this condition. Curbing the cunning tactics of inferior goods being disguised and sold as genuine products depends on these regulations. Now, the government is unwilling to implement even this basic self-imposed regulation and hesitates to act firmly. What hope is there for the future of domestic goods? Alas, weak nations have no diplomacy. Now, even customs administration cannot be managed. Pity the factories, pity the domestic goods industry.

A Chat About Domestic Goods 225

— Wang Shouqiu

Although white sugar cannot be mentioned in the same breath as firewood, rice, oil, salt, soy sauce, vinegar, and tea, it is nevertheless a daily necessity in the household. Because those who enjoy sweets need it constantly, and even those who do not like sweets add a bit when cooking to balance the flavors. Therefore, white sugar has become a necessity in the household.

Our country produces a lot of white sugar, enough to supply the entire nation. However, after Taiwan was ceded to others, white sugar production suddenly decreased. In addition, in recent years, it has suffered from the dumping and squeezing of foreign sugar, causing the domestic sugar industry to decline. In fact, it's not just the sugar industry that's like this; all other industries have suffered from the exclusion of foreign goods and have declined. Furthermore, the Chinese people's habit has always been to conserve what they have and not to research and improve. Therefore, the Chinese white sugar to this day is still not white but yellow. However, although the color is yellow, the taste of the sugar is indeed sweeter than foreign sugar. But although foreign sugar is not very sweet, the color is indeed very white—almost like snow—deserving the name "white sugar." Probably because foreign sugar is snow-white, most people like to buy foreign sugar, so the sales of foreign sugar are very large. According to the statistics of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and the customs, the annual import of foreign sugar reaches 14 million piculs, worth over 10 million yuan, ranking second in the import volume of foreign goods. Look at this number; it is shockingly high! Who would have thought that this small white sugar would have such a huge annual drain, and those who advocate domestic goods have overlooked this item. But now, I urge those who advocate domestic goods to pay attention!

White sugar is said to be made from sugarcane. And in Sichuan and other provinces of our country, because there is too much sugarcane, they dry it and use it as fuel. Isn't this too regrettable? —See the Sichuan investigation by Mr. Gu Zhizhong and others—Hopefully, the great industrialists of our country will pay attention to it, so that the sugar industry of our country can be revived and there will be no more of this huge drain, which is what the people of the country hope and expect day and night!

In addition to foreign sugar, there is another kind of drain that is also considerable. What is it? It's Wrigley's chewing gum. According to the investigation by the Ministry of Industry, there is an annual drain of more than two million yuan. And Shanghai accounts for half of it—one million yuan—Tianjin has about 200,000 yuan, and Beiping has about 120,000 yuan. The rest are sold in Hankou and other ports.—And Guangzhou Province, Fujian Province, and the southwestern provinces are not included in the statistics.—Imagine that this extremely small Wrigley's chewing gum has so much drain every year. This must be thanks to those fashionable men and women!

Let's start advocating domestic goods from these trivial things, compatriots! Work hard! Work hard!

Three Different People 226

— Ke Ding'an

Now there are three different people; please examine them:

A: wears a serge long gown and a straight-collared waistcoat made of tribute wool. B: wears a cloth long gown and a straight-collared vest made of tribute wool. C: wears a spring tweed Western-style suit.

These three people represent the most common clothing of our Chinese people, but Western-style suits are not common in rural towns. People wearing long gowns and vests can be said to be the same everywhere.

Furthermore, long gowns, vests, according to the system, have been around for hundreds of years. Their styles can be said to be inherited! Not only inherited, but they can be said to be passed down by ancestors! In the beginning, they were all Chinese silk fabrics, such as Ning silk, spun silk, and damask satin, etc. Wearing them for at least decades. For example, when an old person no longer wants to wear them, they take them to alter and let their son wear them. When the son no longer wants to wear them, they take them to alter and let their grandson wear them. Grandfather and grandson wear them for three generations, and the material has not been worn through. Then they take them to alter and let the grandson's younger brother wear them. This is genuine Chinese goods, worn for decades. What could be more enjoyable?

Now it's different. After making a piece of clothing, one often doesn't wear it for a few months before it has a hole, or the pattern starts to fray, or the color fades. Not to mention not wearing it for decades, it's even difficult to wear it for a year. It is said that these materials that cannot be worn for a year are foreign goods from faraway lands. This is truly unjust! Chinese people should wear durable Chinese goods. Why buy foreign goods that are not durable? There is a reason for this: [People's desire to win is the same everywhere.] Because of this, if one person wears foreign goods and feels proud of it, others will go and look at the style. Later, hundreds, thousands, or tens of thousands of people are like this. Enough, enough. Everyone takes pride in wearing foreign goods, and Chinese goods have no way to go. Gradually, the prices of agricultural products fall, the rural economy collapses, the market is depressed, and unemployment increases. The situation of the endangered and precarious is coming head-on.

Let's examine the three people, A, B, and C:

A: His serge long gown, the serge for the face, is foreign goods, and the camel hair for the lining is Chinese goods. The straight-collared vest made of tribute wool is foreign goods.

B: The cloth long gown is Chinese goods, but his straight-collared vest made of tribute wool is foreign goods.

C: The whole suit is foreign goods.

Judging from the above, they all have some foreign goods. But Chinese serge, tribute wool, and spring tweed are all available. So why not use them? It all depends on one's own change of mind. So why not wear domestic goods? I believe that in the near future, there will be no such different discoveries among the three people. In other words, [everyone uses domestic goods, and there will no longer be three different people, and wherever you look, everyone will be wearing the same domestic goods.]

Will the Women's Domestic Goods Year Be Redeemed? 227

— Meng Zhao

Time flies, and two-thirds of the [Women's Domestic Goods Year] has already passed! This Women's Domestic Goods Year has added a lot of liveliness to this sluggish market, but it is not uncommon to see it being used as a tool for promoting foreign goods in a blatant manner!

The fashionable girls and wealthy wives in the women's world regard money as insignificant and casually pick fashionable goods to buy. After using them for a short time, they discard the old and replace them with new ones, squandering again! If they continue like this for the rest of their lives, hoping for the redemption of the Women's Domestic Goods Year check is like climbing a tree to catch fish! They are only seen generously redeeming for foreigners and even think of themselves as the smartest women. The figures for things like cosmetics, perfume, and chewing gum are astonishing! I hope that the women's world will quickly realize that the money redeemed for foreigners should be turned into domestic goods redemption for the Women's Domestic Goods Year, occupying the most glorious page in the future history of the revival of domestic goods! I hope that the women's world will quickly take action!

Record of Visiting the Completion of the New Tai Kang Factory 228

— Sun Chucheng

The Shanghai Tai Kang Canned Food Company purchased land next to Fenglin Bridge in southern Shanghai to build a new factory. On April 15th, it held a ceremony to celebrate the completion of the new factory and invited guests from all walks of life to visit. Chucheng went there at 9:00 a.m. that day. The colorful archway at the entrance reached the clouds, fully decorated with electric lights, shining brightly. After signing in, I went to the living room. On the wall hung many plaques presented by Chairman Chiang, such as [Enterprise to Save the Country] and Mayor Wu Tiecheng's [Promote Welfare and Industry]. After meeting old friends such as Fang Shiru and having refreshments, I was led by him to visit. The entire factory is divided into management, engineering, and administrative departments. The engineering department includes eleven sections: biscuit manufacturing, machine manufacturing, can manufacturing, canned food manufacturing, candy manufacturing, Western pastry manufacturing, Chinese pastry manufacturing, bread manufacturing, preserved tangerine peel manufacturing, biscuit packaging, candy packaging, and chemical inspection. Workers are divided into permanent and temporary types. There are about 200 permanent workers, whose wages are calculated by work. Temporary workers' wages are determined according to the complexity of the work. Wages are calculated by piece. Both men and women are employed. When working, male workers wear blue cloth uniforms, and female workers wear white cloth cheongsams, clean and tidy, which is rarely seen in food factories. In the canned food manufacturing department, bamboo baskets are piled up like mountains, and dozens of female workers are unpacking

Words That Can't Be Cried Out 229

— Chu Jianping

Wearing a stiff, foreign lead-skinned Western suit, entering a grand department store, taking out a textured leather wallet, and saying the name of an item in English to the clerk; how imposing and magnificent!

If you want to instantly become a comical figure, just shout "Half a catty of Huadiao wine" or "A bottle of Yuanliang liquor" next to the champagne bottles in any dance hall. It will guarantee you a standing ovation.

Yesterday, on Yuyuan Road in the Town God Temple, I saw a gentleman in loose robes buying a squeaking rubber kitten from a black market peddler. "Is this a Japanese product?" The patriotic gentleman asked.

"It's clearly printed in English on it, so of course it's a British product." The black market peddler pointed to "Made in Japan" as proof.

This gentleman was probably afraid of revealing his ignorance of English and being scolded as a boor by everyone. So he pretended to be an expert and bought one.

The bamboo shoots are cut into strips and placed in a four-foot-high, five-foot-square cement container. After seasoning, they are cooked in a pot. I said to Mr. Fang, "Qin Shaoyou's poem about bamboo shoots says, 'The beautiful color is as lovely as jade cut with a knife, and the pure fragrance is endless as a dragon is cooked in a tripod.' Today, we are here watching young female workers cut so many fresh bamboo shoots with knives and cook them in huge pots. It can be said that we have feasted our eyes. If Shaoyou saw it, I don't know how he would dance with joy." After cooking, they are put into cans and placed on a conveyor belt, automatically transported to the steaming room, which is very convenient. After looking at all the departments, the biscuit-making machine is the most magnificent and interesting. First, there is a machine that mixes flour, milk, white sugar, and other ingredients, rotating endlessly, evenly weighing. Then, there is a machine that cuts the flour mixture into blocks, about one and a half feet wide, two feet long, and one inch high, continuously. The flour blocks are transported to the front machine, pressed into thin sheets one minute high, connected to each other. At first glance, it looks like a bolt of white cloth. Rolling to the front, the machine presses down and prints patterns on the dough, cutting it into round or square shapes, and leaving it on iron plates. It then enters the oven, which is one zhang wide, five zhang long, and six chi high, with three fire doors. The surroundings are built with white porcelain bricks, and the hot air rises without leaking out. After baking, it is poured into bamboo containers and transported to the packaging department by elevator. It is said that this machine was newly purchased from the UK in 1933. With rapid production, the cost can be reduced. To compete with foreign goods, we have to work hard like this. I deeply admire the factory's officers and am happy to record it.

Contributing Opinions

Promote Domestic Goods - Build Hankou - A Free City for the Country 230

— Zhang Yanxiang

Hankou was originally the second largest commercial port in our country, but now it has been reduced to the sixth largest commercial port, falling behind Guangzhou and Tianjin. Looking at Hankou's position, it is still the center of our country's hinterland, but it has declined due to the influence of various environments. One reason is that the Longhai Railway extends to Haizhou in the east and Tongguan in the west, so goods from Shaanxi, Gansu, Shanxi, and Henan provinces all travel east via the Longhai Railway, bypassing Hankou. Second, the shipping on the Sichuan River and Xiang River is developed, and ships from Chongqing, Yisha, Changsha, and Yuekou directly reach Beijing and Shanghai, without transshipment in Hankou. Third, the Yangtze River waterway has not been dredged, and it is becoming increasingly shallow, while the Xiang River is silting up year by year, making it difficult for goods to flow smoothly and reducing exports. This is based on transportation. Other disasters caused by soldiers and bandits and the loss of the Northeast are important reasons for Hankou's decline. Now, people generally believe that the revival of Hankou will be when the Zhushao section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway is completed, and the entire line is open to traffic, when it can regain the commercial leader in Central China and hold the transportation hub between the North and the South. I don't think so. The Guangdong-Hankou Railway is expected to be open to traffic in four years, and the Yuping Railway is also being built. In the future, goods from Yunnan, Guangxi, Hunan, and Guizhou will definitely be transferred to the Yuping Railway in Zhuzhou and travel east to Shanghai and Hangzhou, which is faster and more convenient than transferring to river ships in Hankou. If the future Eastern port can be completed, this route will be even shorter than traveling down the Yangtze River. Therefore, when the Guangdong-Hankou Railway and the Yuping Railway are completed at the same time, the Hankou market will have no benefit. Moreover, when the Guangdong-Hankou Railway is completed, the Wuhan Railway Bridge has not yet been built. The river surface is vast, and the tide rises and falls about fifty feet. Even if a train ferry is set up across the river, it will be much more difficult than between Nanjing and Pukou and difficult to achieve in a short time. Therefore, goods coming north from the southern section will stop in Wuchang and cannot reach Hankou. Furthermore, judging from the terrain of Hankou, the areas along the river are mostly tidal flats, accumulating silt and sand, making it difficult to moor large ships. In the future, unloading docks and warehouses will be mostly set up on the Wuchang side, and Hankou will only remain a commercial market. Hankou's terrain is low-lying and humid. The northwest sides are blocked by railways. Outside the railways, there is no market at all. East of the railways, there is only an extremely narrow area, which is already crowded and difficult to expand. In the future, factories will definitely be set up less in Hankou.

According to the above observations, it is fundamentally difficult to revive the Hankou market, which will further hinder the promotion of domestic goods. Because the Hankou market is not developed, the industry will not prosper. Industrial products rely solely on imports from other ports, and the market will be even more impoverished. Moreover, the imported industrial products and consumables are all foreign goods. Domestic industrial products and consumables from Shanghai, Nanjing, and Jiujiang cannot come to Hankou either. Foreign goods rely on the protection of their tariffs. When transported from Shanghai to Hankou, they do not need to pay taxes again. Domestic goods manufactured in Shanghai have already paid tariffs on imported raw materials and coal. When their products are transported to Hankou, they have to pay tariffs again, which is actually a double taxation system and a reverse protection tax system that protects foreign goods and encroaches on the domestic goods market. (To be continued)

Worth Introducing Domestic Pediatric Medicine Partridge Vegetable 232

Foreign pediatric pills sell in large numbers in the domestic market every year, which is alarming. The owner of Guangzhou Hongxing Pharmacy, seeing this, invented a kind of partridge vegetable, in order to stop this drain. The medicine is mild and effective, and it is good for treating all kinds of children's diseases and also helps children grow. Children from one to eleven years old, suffering from malnutrition, worm infestation, milk regurgitation, night crying, epilepsy, stomach pain, headache, abdominal distension, constipation, teeth grinding after sleeping, sallow complexion, thinness, etc., all kinds of miscellaneous diseases, once taken, the effect is miraculous. It is truly a sacred medicine for children. The price is low, and the method of administration is simple, requiring only half a cup of boiled water to brew it. It is even better than other kinds of pills and powders. It has been sold in South China for many years. Everyone in Guangzhou, Siam, Annam, Singapore, and the Philippines knows the effect of partridge vegetable and regards it as a family secret treasure. The box surface is printed with a portrait of the inventor Zhang Siyun, and the printing is exquisite. Now, in order to facilitate patients in this city and North China, we have entrusted Changfaxing in Huayefang, Jiujiang Road, to be the sole agent.

Homecoming 234

— Lin Huiyin

Because I had to catch the train, I got up earlier than I had in two years. The train was leaving at nine o'clock, and I arrived in Suzhou a little after eleven. I got into a rickshaw, but because I didn't know where to go, I asked it to stop when it reached Quanmen Road.

But do I really not know where to go? No, it's not that I don't know, it's just that I'm hesitating. Although I've wanted to go see Miss -- for so long, now that I'm really in Suzhou, I can't decide whether to go see her or not.

Regarding Miss --, I've heard several people praise her in front of me. Afterwards, I paid attention to her articles -- they were indeed not bad, and I read several of her lectures. The good thing about her articles is that they are not pretentious, whether they are written by a literati or a woman. So I always wanted to go see her, but I couldn't find an excuse to go see her. I was embarrassed to tell my family that I ran to Suzhou specifically to see her, and I wouldn't even do that to myself. That would seem too formal, at least in her eyes. And I had never gone to see someone I didn't know like that, and without an introduction. For her, I decided: either don't go, or if I go, I definitely won't use an introduction. I was just waiting for the excuse to come. And finally, it came, which was the wedding of one of my relatives. So I decided to personally offer my congratulations. On the night before I left, I got her address from an editor over the phone, although I didn't hear it very clearly.

[I've wanted to go see her for so long, why don't I go see her?] I asked myself as I walked.

[-- Bay? Do you know -- Garden?] I finally blurted out to a rickshaw puller who was trying to get my business [--- Garden? I know it. It's --- Garden.]

[Where is it?] I was a little distrustful. [Inside -- Gate.]

That's right, I heard -- Gate clearly. The rickshaw puller asked me to stop and wait for him to pull the rickshaw over.

[I don't want it now; I have to eat something.] I was still hesitating. I gave him a few copper coins and didn't want his rickshaw.

[I can wait while you eat,] he said stubbornly, recommending this restaurant and that dim sum shop.

I still refused him and just walked on my own.

But after I had eaten my dim sum and came out of a shop, still not very sure, I saw the rickshaw puller squatting on the footboard of his rickshaw, waiting. As soon as he saw me, he stood up and let me get into the rickshaw.

And so, I was taken to the door of Miss --'s house without any trouble, thanks to the rickshaw puller's persistence.

As I got out of the rickshaw, I saw a young lady ringing the doorbell. I thought it was her, so I told her who I was looking for. She said she was at home; the door opened, and she guided me to sit in the living room.

Soon, Miss -- came out. [Oh, Mr. Lin, we've met,] she said with a smile as she stepped through the door of the living room. (To be continued)

Regarding Children 235

— Da Ye

The boys were idle and looking for something to do for fun. They were tired of many old toys, so they said, "Let's do literature!" Then A-Da wiped his snot and wrote a novel. A-Er threw aside his rubber ball and said, "If you write a novel, I'll critique it!" A-San said, "I smoke cigarettes, so I'll do cigarette literature!" A-Xi said, "I heard a joke yesterday, so I'll tell jokes!" The little girl Xiao-Mao was holding a pencil and drawing flowers on drawing paper, muttering, "You're all doing literature, so I'll do art!" So, for a while, they all buried themselves at their desks and worked hard.

The adults heard that the children were all quiet and were very surprised. They looked and saw that they were all buried at their desks, so they said, "Let them play! Just don't make a scene in the market..."

Moreover, with such a comparison, the adults and gentlemen will again be unhappy! But please don't look down on children! Isn't "Ren Jian Shi" (The Human World) a famous chapter in Zhuangzi? Taking the book of Zhuangzi as an example, its ultimate state of inaction is probably returning to one's original state and transforming into a child. Zhuangzi is consistent with Laozi. Laozi does not oppose "infants". Most of those in the world who dislike infants are Buddhists. In the Shingon sect, "fearless infant mind", "fasting mind of a foolish child" and "heart of a different-born ram" are listed together. But this doesn't matter. The master of humor does not believe in Buddhism.

It seems that today we advocate humor, tomorrow we advocate smoking, and the day after tomorrow we oppose phlegm-filled poems (although I myself reluctantly echoed an old man in a poem, which is not necessarily free of phlegm). Suddenly, we discover that the essay is the orthodox form of literature! -- (This is like a prodigal son suddenly finding a small pearl in a broken cabinet and shouting, "This is still worth something!") Alas! This is why this "Daoist brother" is a "child"!

"If you want to walk the great path, do not show the small paths; do not contain the great sea in a cow's footprint, do not equate the sunlight with a firefly"! Therefore, acting as a benevolent and righteous person, wearing out the crown of one's head and wearing out one's heels, although it may not be kept secret, but sitting in the Yellow River breach and still feeling complacent will inevitably make people feel sad. If we are advocating, it is more meaningful to advocate greater things! Is the success of essays in the past fourteen years the result of advocating essays? Or is it the result of advocating Western culture, which is a thousand times greater than essays?

Bookstores don't sell Western literature books; they are competing to produce children's textbooks and toys. Sellers and buyers are both saving effort. In the remaining mountains and rivers, only "children" like a crowd of monkeys can be accommodated, unable to do anything and unwilling to do anything. To save society, only humor and essays are left. Encourage them!

How to Read Zhou Zuoren's Poetry 236

— Lin Yutang

Recently, someone who has not yet achieved fame, in Ren Yan Zhou Kan, Ten Days Talk, Contradiction Monthly, China Daily and Free Talk, using pseudonyms to contribute articles, has systematically attacked "Ren Jian Shi". It is like a wild fox discussing Buddhism or a leper discussing immortality. I don't want to argue. But there was another article in Free Talk criticizing Mr. Zhou Zuoren's personal attitude. Today, after reading Mr. Cao Juren's "Mr. Zhou Zuoren's Self-Congratulatory Poem," it resonates deeply with my heart, and I feel I have something to say. Yesterday, I received a draft from Mr. Zhou and Ren Jian Shi, with a short note attached: "I received a letter from Mr. Liu Dajie, who said that reading my clumsy poem made him shed tears with sadness. I greatly admire this kind of interpretation." (The original letter has been forwarded to Mr. Liu, so this is a summary of its main points). I replied to Mr. Zhou's letter. Although I have no copy, the gist is as follows... This poem is certainly meant to be interpreted in this way, expressing deep sorrow through leisure. But there are too many vulgar people in the world, and there has been much criticism from the outside. I can listen to it, but I only blame myself for not publishing this poem, placing it before the eyes of boors and fools. Changju and Jieni were passionate people in the world. The Ming people had some sayings...

The so-called saying of the Ming people comes from Xu Fang's reply to Fu Yingbin's letter, which is recorded here:

I am inherently shallow and narrow-minded, and I am also ignorant and unenlightened about the affairs of the current world. I have always been garrulous and loquacious, not daring to claim that I am lonely and radical, but also because in the battle within the same room, righteousness dictates that I cannot sit idly by. In the end, what good does a hair's breadth do? It only adds another crime. To strangle a jackal's throat and snatch its food, the thought is urgent, but those with knowledge will laugh at its foolishness. It has always been like this. Not just today. Moreover, Chu Kuang and Jieni are the coldest people in the Spring and Autumn period. However, tasting their words, they are not the cold people of the world, but precisely the hot people of the world. It is extremely hot, and there is nothing to be done, so one has to return to coldness. Extreme heat must be extreme cold. This is why one sighs on a raft. I have always been most opposed to the theory that pure talk destroyed the Jin Dynasty. The fall of the Jin was not due to Ruan Ji's licentiousness, but to the environment in which昏君 and tyrannical rulers killed people like hemp, forcing Ruan Ji to be licentious. In the past, China had no civil rights, and outspoken scholars often died at the hands of eunuchs. The party imprisonment of the Han Dynasty and the Qing debates of the Ming Dynasty are all examples of this. Later historians often say that pure talk destroyed the country, which is no different from exonerating the rebellious eunuchs. It is crude and also unjust. Drinking and being licentious, or being silent and unknown, is only being clean and self-respecting. Today's lepers want those who are clean and self-respecting to bear the crime of destroying the country. If so, then those who are "today united like crows, tomorrow scattered like crows, today surrendering, tomorrow leaning on the carriage bar, today gentlemen, tomorrow villains, today villains, tomorrow back to gentlemen" can be blameless. Even Confucius, a sage, sighed about floating on the sea on a raft. Today's lepers, with a face full of Confucian indignation, almost want to surpass the sage.

Wan Sheng 237

— Ms. Cao Ming

Wan Sheng, one of my cousins, has round and sparkling black eyes and plump cheeks that often show two dimples. This face, which is both gentle and lively, yet also strong and resilient, constantly endures her wretched circumstances: the vapor machines in the silk factory that broil the blood of the female workers; a father addicted to alcohol who wastes away her youth, and a gambling-crazed brother.

In our village, women occupy the main position in terms of production. Apart from managing silk, cocoons, planting mulberry trees, and working as clerks, the men either idle around or go to the cities. As for the women, their fate is decided from birth: their vitality is either worn down in the silk factory or consumed in the mulberry fields. Our Wan Sheng is similarly tormented by fate; on the one hand, she fully embodies the characteristics of these independent Shunde women—naturally, not every Shunde woman is like this—people who have been close to Shunde women will surely find her courage in her gentleness, and her decisiveness in her liveliness.

When Wan Sheng was twenty-seven or eight years old, I was only half her age. Because my family had said that in another year or two, they would ask me to apprentice with her, I slowly began to pay attention to her.

In the summer, around seven o'clock in the afternoon, Wan Sheng could be found on the highest stone step of a ferry in Dongxi River. She listlessly held her rice bowl, chewing without energy, allowing her weak figure to be reflected on the yellow and turbid river water. Sometimes, she would put down her chopsticks, walk down the stone steps, soak her feet in the water, and stare at the surface of the river with eyes that were both tired and worried.

"I'm going to be your apprentice in the future. Are you happy?" One day, I sat next to her on the stone steps of the ferry and said to her.

"You? Well, I advise you not to enter the silk factory!" She said decisively. "You should change your profession as soon as possible. What good is there in a silk factory? -- It's simply a furnace -- Just think of bones as branches. When the branches are baked dry by the fire and the sap turns into charcoal, they will break with a single knock. Really, we don't dare to use any force when we turn over at night!" She swallowed a mouthful of rice, forcefully made me eat a piece of pork, and continued, "We work hard until late, not to mention the benefits, eating enough and wearing coarse linen clothes is already considered good, but it's impossible! Well, the women here... We've never done anything wrong, and I don't believe in things like committing crimes in a previous life... Jiu Mei, you're young, you don't understand much." I loved listening to her words, which had a bit of the sour and astringent taste of unripe green plums. (To be continued)

Recollections 238

— Bai Yan

Recollections are a thin mist:

- Obscuring your reason.

Making you rejoice;

Making you grieve.

·········

Recollections are a glass of fine wine;

- Paralyzing your nervous system.

Making you intoxicated;

Making you feel lost.

··········

Recollections are a wildfire;

- Burning in your chest.

Making you excited;

Making you mad.

Country Gleanings 239

— Feng Zi

(I) Sound

These past few years, having lived outside for a long time, returning occasionally, I feel a sense of alienation from everything in my hometown. My heart always feels incomplete, as if it's not as intimate as it's stored in my memory. Sometimes, when I think about it, I feel that the seasons are still the same, the scenery is still the same, and nothing has changed.

Like a swallow that has changed its nest, lost, lost.

The Jiaochuan River still flows, and the years flow by in the same way, but the classmates of my youth have all been taken to the cities by the conditions of survival. Here, only some old, young, and female people are left, wealthy local tyrants and gentry, and poor wretches who have no money to go out. With these people, the air here is always only dull. On the one hand, there is exploitation and enjoyment, and on the other hand, there is the so-called "making a living by chewing on bitter juice."

Exerting all one's strength to practice extreme suppression, and exerting all one's strength to endure extreme suppression, forms this silent village.

The countryside is truly "silent." If there is any sound, it is the sound of firecrackers at the Lunar New Year, but after this period, one no longer hears it. Now, perhaps only the elderly have a weak lament for the ways of the world and the human heart! But what kind of sound does this make?

The children grow up year by year, batch after batch running to the cities. The countryside can only remain a longing in their minds forever. Those who remain are mostly under the age of ten. But children under the age of ten will still grow up and still run to the cities.

After how much longer, the countryside will probably become an area without strong men! Even women, many go to the bustling cities to work or as helpers, but most of them still remain here.

The lamentations of the elderly have never had a progressive effect on this village. The women do not even have a lament. They only know how to find a way to ensure that they are warm and full for this one day. When they can't be warm and full, they say that they were born with this bitter fate.

The women in our area do not do the work in the fields; at most, they only grow some vegetables. Therefore, apart from the money that the men can send back from the cities, the women's ways of making a living are only to work as seamstresses, sell vegetables, or raise a few chickens to sell eggs. During the day, they are not satisfied, and they look for some indoor work at night. Even after midnight, when even the sound of dogs is silent, one can still often hear the "swishing" sound of spinning yarn.

This must be the only sound that replaces their mouths!

Huaiyang Folk Song 240

— Yang Sheng

Yesterday, the west wind blew yellow sand, opening the curtain and seeing her; Narrow waist and tiny feet, pink face like peach blossoms. Selling acres of fields,

Pawning a car; Marrying the dear enemy home early, So I don't have to worry about both sides, So you don't have to worry about both sides!

Mom (7) 241

— Luo Hong

Father and Li Gu turned around, ready to leave. My younger sister was still grumbling, "I want to go too..." But they left without looking back. Li Gu was still smiling and saying something to Father, and Father nodded. In the child's heart, this was really too sad. Why wouldn't Father agree? Moreover, they blamed Li Gu for their complaints about Father. If she had said a word, he might have agreed, but Li Gu didn't say a word. The sadness made the older brother cry, and then the younger sister also cried. He complained a lot about Father. He had said before that he would play with them for two days, but he was only playing for one day. Dad was really not a good dad. He was so happy to go with Li Gu, but why wouldn't he take them? Li Gu would only smile and wouldn't say a kind word. If it were Mom, she would definitely take them! Dad also said that Li Gu would love them... The more he thought about it, the more pitiful he felt, and the more tears he shed. The younger sister cried and shouted:

"Brother, Dad won't take us, we won't go to school tomorrow, we'll ask Lu Ma to take us to play!"

The older brother was still crying and didn't answer his younger sister's words. It took a lot of effort from Lu Ma and Wang Ma to coax him inside. "I want Mom!" He stopped crying and stomped his feet, saying. He looked at the mother's photo and cried again.

At bedtime, the younger sister pouted and said:

"Brother, Li Gu won't take us, I don't like her."

The older brother looked at her and said:

"Li Gu doesn't love us!"

The children were all asleep. In his sleep, the older brother saw his mother holding his younger sister. His mother was telling her fairy tales, and his younger sister was leaning in his mother's arms, swaying gently. He was playing with a rubber ball alone, and his mother called out to him, "Ming, your ball is so dirty, come and listen to Mom's story!" So he stopped and listened for a while. His mother smiled and swayed, constantly telling the story. Suddenly, his younger sister interrupted his mother's story and said:

"Mom, what snacks are we eating?"

"Ah, Mom didn't make any today, be a good girl and listen to the story!"

"I want some!" The younger sister's little hand gently stroked Mom's face.

So Mom took out many beautiful soft candies and biscuits from the drawer and distributed them to them. But when he turned around, Mom was gone, so he shouted loudly for Mom and looked everywhere. It seemed that Mom was answering him and hugging him, but when he opened his eyes, it was Dad who was hugging him! "Wake up, Ming, don't cry, Dad is hugging you!"

But when the child heard his words, he cried even more fiercely.

"Mom is gone, I want Mom!" he shouted.

"Dad is here, don't cry!" Father said, and a tear fell on the child's cheek.

"Mom is gone!" The child lay on his father's shoulder, sobbing sadly. (The End)

The Main Reason for the Sudden Boom in North China Sales: Some Prices Are Lower Than Japanese Yarn; High Cotton Prices Affect Chinese Factories Reducing Work and Shipping 254

Since September 18th, the North China cotton yarn market has been completely occupied by Japanese yarn, leaving no room for Chinese yarn. This has caused a major blow to China's cotton industry. Near Wheat Down, Far Wheat Up 257

Yesterday's wheat market showed a trend of near decline and far stability for each month. Foreign wheat quotations continued to be lower by a small 1-2 corners, so market sentiment was naturally uneasy. However, at present, the highs and lows are temporarily distinguished between near and far. Because this month is the last day of trading, there is a lot of inventory on the market, and factories have no intention of receiving, so the bulls are under actual pressure and have to shout down. The distant months, although initially average, later turned brisk due to the flour market turning brisk and because off-market longs gradually increased. It is said to be related to those who hold up flour prices, so market sentiment has also improved slightly. However, the wheat market must recently look at the weather and the annual harvest, and it cannot be compared with the flour market situation. As a result, the current month fell another 5 points, and the closing price was miserably small at 3 yuan and 83 corners. June rose by 3 points, July rose by 5 points, and August rose by 3 points. Spot wheat has not opened because the factory's stomach has not moved.

Shashi Rough Rice Continues Up Great Five Cents 258

Yesterday, the arrival of Ke Hsien rice from various places was small. The Ke group's appetite was very strong. However, for several consecutive days, the two major groups from Fuzhou and the mainland have been conducting business smoothly. The market price has gradually increased. The arrival is small, and the cargo owners have shouted loudly. The entering households claim greatly and are unwilling to yield. Therefore, the volume of transactions has decreased. Only the yarn market Hsien rice is being competed for by the Fuzhou group and the mainland. Yesterday, 1,500 bags were traded, and the price increased by another 5-6 points. The general market price opened at 5 yuan and 8 corners, and the next was 5 yuan and 7 corners. The prices of other various shaking machine rice and small twisted rice have all stabilized. A total of 3,296 bags of various rice were shipped out of the city, and were divided among this street, Fuzhou, and the mainland. If there are no smooth sales in the future, the market price may temporarily stabilize again.

(South Shanghai) The sources for various groups have slightly increased again, with nearly 50 numbers arriving (over 8,000 stones). Late rice accounts for about half, and the distribution situation is bleak. The Rong group's purchase appetite continues to be strong. For example, the North and South Ocean groups have been quite active since the beginning. The situation seems to feel stagnant, but later the arrival sources also surged. Therefore, although the sellers once shouted up the price, the customers' eating plate was difficult to loosen in the end. Soybeans Sell Smoothly and Prices Rise 260

The soybean market price continued to rise yesterday by 3-4 cents or so. The price of goods from Zhongguan was fresher and more attractive than high-quality beans, so the sentiment was good. The distribution situation included factories trading 7-8 carts of Yingzhou beans, priced from 2 yuan and 62 cents to 56 cents, and also going to Dangshan beans for one cart, priced at 2 yuan and 60 cents. Local purchasing agents purchased 3 carts of large-grained Yingzhou beans, priced from 2 yuan and 65 cents to 63 cents, and also going to Feihe beans for two carts, priced at 2 yuan and 68 cents to 66 cents. Export groups purchased two carts of Zhengyangguan beans, priced from 2 yuan and 74 cents to 77 cents. The arrival source is still not surging, and is currently around 10 carts per day. There may not be much more in the future, so the future of the soybean market has a fairly stable foothold.

Silk and Tea - Spring Cold Affects Silkworm Development 261

Early Spring Chill Affects Silkworm Ant Development. [Yuhang] The collection of early silkworm ants this season is uneven. Late silkworms are better. After the leaves opened, the weather was clear and warm, and silkworm development was smooth. Unexpectedly, after continuous spring rains, coupled with colder weather, the early gang of silkworms with three sleeps and vigorous leaves, due to unsuitable temperature and humidity, were found to have diseases such as not eating and not sleeping. The late silkworms' third sleep was also not working, and silkworm households are busy taking care of them. [Yuanjiachang] Farmers in the area are quite happy to raise ants this year. However, there are more people raising late silkworms. After collecting the ants, the weather was clear and warm, and the silkworms developed quite well. In the past two days, the spring cold was severe, and combined with the uncoordinated feeding of leaves after the rain, most of the early silkworms were stiff and unable to get up, and the late silkworms' appetite also decreased sharply. The instructors are currently adjusting the temperature, and the silkworm households have all set up fire basins in the silkworm room to increase warmth and remove humidity. [Shangyu] Farmers in the four villages all incubated the improved species distributed by the Improvement Association this year. The weather was clear and warm during the incubation period, and the collection of ants was quite uniform, and the development was also good. Most of the large gangs have already completed two sleeps and have sufficient leaves. Unexpectedly, it has been raining heavily for the past two days, and the weather has suddenly turned cold. The silkworms are delaying their sleep, and everyone is using firepower to get warm. [Haiyan] Silkworm households in various cities and villages have reduced the amount of feeding this year because they have learned from previous years' silkworm failures, and have discarded native silkworm species and did not raise them. They all hatched improved species, and the instructors helped to promote the green. The early gangs have been opening leaves for the first sleep for many days, and the late gangs have also tried the leaves. Fortunately, the instructors fed them with improved mulberry leaves, so although the weather is cold and rainy, the impact is still slight.

Waste Silk Transportation Methods Are Increasingly Sparse. Our country's yellow and white silk heads (collectively referred to as waste silk by the customs) have traditionally relied on French sales as the destination. In recent years, the impact of artificial silk and Japanese silk scraps (i.e., silk heads) has caused French sales to plummet. This time, the French mail ship Xue Xianghao exported only 89 packages of yellow and white silk heads jointly owned by Baili and others to Marseilles and other ports.

Factory Classics Only Have Spot Trading. Recently, the foreign exchange rate has gradually shrunk, and silk prices are looking good. However, the European and American markets currently have thick silk inventories, and the supply exceeds demand, so factory sales have not improved. Although Chinese silk has a higher pulling price due to the reduced exchange rate, the light factories in Shanghai have spot transactions, estimating that yesterday B had 20 but the price turned firm.

The Upcoming Release of Zhuji Green Tea 262

In Zhuji, Xiaoshan, and other areas of Zhejiang Province, which are traditionally known for producing the earliest batches of green tea, the tea buds have been slow to develop due to the recent cold weather, barely showing their tips. According to people from the area, tea farmers in Zhuji are preparing to begin picking tea leaves immediately. However, buyers are showing little interest, so the price of the new tea is not expected to be high.

There are still 6,000 boxes of tea stored in Shanghai. New tea will soon be on the market. According to a recent survey, there are still over 6,100 boxes of tea stored in Shanghai, including 5,400 boxes of local "Zhen Mei," "Zhen Mei Needle," and "Xiu Mei" green teas, and only 700 boxes of imported green tea. The future trend of the tea market is most unfavorable for local teas.

News from Anhui Province on the Eve of Tea Harvesting 263

Wuyuan green tea is considered the highest grade among foreign boxed teas. It is regarded as an unparalleled treasure in European and American markets. In recent years, while Russian sales of "Gong Xi" tea have declined, the demand for other varieties such as "Zhen Mei," "Chou Xin," "Feng Mei," "Xiu Mei," "Zhen Mei Needle," "Ma Zhu," "Gong Zhu," "Zhi Zhu," and "Xia Mu" teas has steadily increased in various European and American countries. Therefore, in the competition among foreign teas, Wuyuan tea's reputation remains unshakable. In recent years, affected by the global economic panic, sales have decreased compared to previous years, but prices are still higher than before the tenth year of the Republic [1921]. Last year, those who sold their tea early and quickly made a small profit, while those who held on to it suffered losses. This year, existing tea businesses, noting that the tea stored in Shanghai has been sold and that foreign demand remains strong, are continuing to operate. The demand for supplies such as crates, firewood, charcoal, lead strips, and paper has increased as tea businesses rush to prepare. As of now, except for tea businesses in the southwest villages bordering Jiangxi, which have been disrupted by local communist bandits and cannot open, about 200 tea businesses in the three northeastern towns are preparing to open. This has created a palpable sense of tension in the market.

Liuan and Huoshan are renowned tea-producing areas in western Anhui. Areas such as Mabuxi, Hujiadian, Qingshan, Maotanchang, Guanjia Du, Du Bo, Lianhua Shan, and Fenghuang Tai all produce excellent tea. The annual output is approximately 400,000 [units of measurement]. Local shops and businesses specialize in teas categorized by shape, such as "Mao Jian," "Xiang Pian," "Lian Xin," "Que She," "Gua Pian," "Que Zhen," "Mei Pian," "Kui Zhen," "Yu Zhen," "Yin Zhen," and "Feng Chi." The largest market is Shandong Province, followed by North China and other provinces. However, due to years of banditry, tea merchants have been hesitant to travel to the area, and sales have declined year by year. This spring's tea market is particularly sluggish. Stored tea sells for only three or four yuan per [unit of measurement], and those priced at five or six yuan are rarely inquired about. Business is 70-80% lower than in previous years. Tea farmers generally feel the hardship of having goods they cannot sell. With the spring rains, the new tea season is about to begin. The bandits near Qingshan and the Taojia River area have not yet been suppressed. The Huoshan County Magistrate, recognizing that the livelihoods of the local people depend entirely on tea, has, in conjunction with the Tea Industry Association, telegraphed the Chairman of Anhui Province, requesting the dispatch of troops to be stationed in the tea-producing areas to protect merchants conducting business and to aid the rural areas. At present, tea merchants from Shandong are gradually arriving, but not with the same enthusiasm as in the past. The prospects for this year's tea market are still difficult to predict.

Sugar Market: White Sugar Rises with Customs Gold Unit 264

Yesterday, the sugar market was tense due to the sharp rise in the Customs Gold Unit to 2042. Spot prices, such as No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar, rose by 20 cents to 20.02 yuan. No. 9 KNG red sugar was priced at 15.80 yuan, and local No. 1 refined white sugar was priced at 18.60 yuan, also up 10 cents, with transactions occurring. However, Swire Sugar's "B" mark, although quoted at 20.05 yuan, saw no transactions. Wholesalers offered over a hundred boxes of Beihai "Pian Qing" sugar from Guangdong at 9 yuan, and over a hundred packages of Longjiang "Qing" sugar from Chaozhou at 10.40 yuan. Several dozen packages of "Zhi Yang" sugar were offered at 15 yuan, and over eighty packages of "Tong Shou Hu Ru Fen" sugar were offered at 7.50 yuan. A Jianbang wholesaler offered sixty packages of No. 2 and 3 Guangbing sugar at the original price of 24 yuan, but buyers were uninterested, and no transaction occurred.

Metals: Crude Lead Estimated at Sixteen Yuan 265

Since the sharp decline in foreign exchange rates, metal prices have soared. Wholesale prices have reached 15.75 yuan per picul, an increase of 15 cents from the previous day, while retail prices have reached 16 yuan, an increase of over 30 cents. Tea merchants are very eager to purchase, resulting in transactions of two to three hundred bars.

Essays

National Crisis and National Self-Salvation 266

— Gu She

The nation is now at a critical juncture, a moment of imminent peril. Japan is manipulating China at will, and the tension of the international imperialist struggle in the Far East has reached an unprecedented peak. At this moment, China has truly become "meat on the chopping block, to be carved up at will." Fellow citizens! Do you also feel that we are facing an "imminent disaster"?

Looking back to the September 18th Incident [Mukden Incident] and its aftermath, our national spirit was initially so tense. Anti-Japanese associations, volunteer armies, petitions, and demonstrations, almost everyone's blood was stirred, and they engaged in the national salvation movement. They ran around calling for help, with extreme enthusiasm. But now, there is silence. As the national crisis intensifies day by day, the people's passion for national salvation is declining day by day. What kind of phenomenon is this? This is a true sign of national demise! The national crisis is not as worrying as the people's decadence, which has reached such a degree that it is more than enough to lead to the country's downfall!

Fellow citizens, do not think that because we have been shouting about "national demise" and "national demise" for decades, and have been hearing about "joint administration" and "partition" for so long, but the country has not yet fallen, has not yet been "jointly administered," and has not yet been "partitioned," that we will still be able to get through this, no matter how severe the crisis is, so there is no need to rush. This is the biggest mistake, the most irreparable psychology of national demise! You must know that the reason why we have not been "partitioned" or "jointly administered" in the past, and the country has not nominally fallen, is not because we have the ability to survive on our own, but because they have not yet found it necessary to move from de facto partition and joint administration to de jure partition and joint administration. That is to say, they do not need to immediately implement de jure partition or joint administration. There is still a balance of power between them, and they can rely on this balance of power to peacefully and equally exploit China. But now, things are very different. The balance of power in the Far East has long been broken by Japan's September 18th actions. On the one hand, the intensification of the imperialist crisis has also forced them to intensify the division of colonies. By the end of the 19th century, the world's colonies had already been completely divided. After the World War of 1914-1918, there was a second allocation, and now the only country left is China. Although China has already been de facto allocated to various powers, it nominally maintains independence. Now, what they are discussing is how to move from de facto partition to de jure partition. Everyone simply divides a piece of land in China, marks it with the name of a certain country, and sends a governor-general to administer it. And Japan was the first to implement this plan. Following Japan's example, other countries will inevitably "follow suit." This has led to the recent fierce competition among the powers for China. The result of the struggle for China will naturally and easily lead to China's demise, from de facto to de jure, directly belonging to various countries. This is an inevitable path. You must know that this is the inevitable result of the development of imperialism to its final stage! As the imperialist crisis develops to its [missing word] point, the division of colonies becomes more [missing word], and this division [missing word] will not stop until the final fall of imperialist justice. Fellow citizens, should you all clearly recognize the deepening of this crisis?

As the struggle between imperialist powers intensifies day by day, the degree of China's partition also increases day by day. It is believed that in the near future, the magic hands of imperialism will extend to China and truly tear our map into pieces. Fellow citizens, do you all feel that the degree of this crisis has reached a terrible peak? Decadence and enjoyment cannot save our souls! Arise! Awaken early and work together to find a way to save ourselves!

Thorough Understanding of China 267

— Meng Ruo

This can be considered a kind of glory. Our country has always only had students going abroad to study, but now Japan has sent children to study in our country. A Reuters dispatch from the 15th stated: "The East Asian Common Culture Association has selected ten young boys from Japan and sent them to study in China. These students are scheduled to depart from Tokyo Station at 10:00 AM on the 22nd of this month and travel to Kobe, where they will take a connecting ship to China on the 25th. The ages of these boys, including Inoue Shinichi, are all 14. Seven of them will go to Tianjin to study at the Sino-Japanese College, while the remaining three are scheduled to enter the Jianghan Middle School in Hankou. They also plan to take the entrance exams for Chinese universities in the future. They are scheduled to study for ten years, followed by six years of compulsory service, so that they can thoroughly understand China."

Sending students to study abroad is a very common thing and not worth making a fuss about. But the actions of the Japanese always have a bit of mystery, making it difficult to fathom their depths. For example, this time they want to send people to our country to study, but the purpose is not to seek knowledge, but to thoroughly understand China. Isn't there an intention here? Could it be that they are constantly clamoring for Sino-Japanese friendship, but they do not understand the situation in our country, and must wait for these ten handsome young boys selected from all over Japan to understand it after ten years? No, they have added the word "thoroughly" to their understanding. It turns out that they do understand China, but their understanding is not thorough enough. Therefore, this time they have specially sent these Japanese children to study, hoping that they will be able to thoroughly understand our country in the future. When I first heard this news, I couldn't help but feel a mixture of sadness and joy. The sad thing is that before Japan has thoroughly understood our country, we have already lost a huge piece of land. If they thoroughly understand it one day, I am afraid that our old and big China will not be able to be preserved. The happy thing is that perhaps the reason why Japan has always bullied our country is because they have not thoroughly understood our country. Fortunately, they will thoroughly understand it in the future, and will return the lost territory to us and truly treat us with the warmth of brothers. Fortunately, these ten young Japanese men are about to come to our country, and we may as well temporarily entrust the fate of our country to them!

Speaking of students studying abroad, it has stirred up many feelings in us. Doesn't our country also send batches of students to Europe, America, or Japan every year to study? And aren't there also many students who return from Europe, America, or Japan every year? But what they bring to us is something we really can't say. Among them, I don't know if there is anyone who can thoroughly understand foreign countries? Perhaps they always understand a lot, because students from our country have always had a common tendency. If he studied in the United States, after returning home, he would advocate pro-Americanism. If he studied in England or Japan, after returning home, he would advocate pro-British or pro-Japaneseism. If they didn't thoroughly understand, how could they advocate friendship with others? What's more, there are those who advocate national betrayal. Those traitors and flattering factions that have emerged in our country recently were all studying in Japan before. According to this reasoning, these few Japanese teenagers who have come to China to study with important missions [missing word] after returning from their studies, will probably not be [missing word] to our country [missing word]. We will wait [missing word]! We would like to express some welcome to them in advance!

A Letter That Cannot Be Delivered to XX 270

— Guanghan

Are you still in this world? It's been almost a year since we received your letter! At first, we suspected that you had been squeezed out of the bureau, because we were always worried that your small position would be difficult to maintain. And you once told me that even if your superiors were willing to accommodate you, that world of demons and monsters was not a place for you to settle down, and it would be better to go back to your hometown and eat sweet potatoes. But, people would definitely inform us if they left A Port and went elsewhere, but we have not yet received any news from you about this [missing word]. Or have you seen through that we are friends who are ungrateful and lack loyalty, not worthy of sharing hardships, so you angrily decided to break off relations with us? You are poor, how can we not know deeply. Having to treat a guest to three copper coins worth of peanuts, I once swallowed white rice mixed with tears in the dark! But after we fled, you should be able to imagine the difficult and arduous situation. Without you asking for help, we have tried our best several times to scrape together some money to send to you, but we are powerless to do so, and the regrets in our hearts are never remedied for the hunger in your stomachs! Oh, perhaps our speculation is wrong? Are you such a person?

Or are you truly unfortunate and have died? In the last letter you wrote to us, from the hasty and crooked handwriting and the intermittent and plaintive sentences, we know that your illness was unusually rapid and severe! What makes us feel infinitely shocked and sad is that there are still faint traces of your tears and bloodstains on the letter paper! After reading this bad news, we couldn't help but look at each other in dismay! What disease are you suffering from? The letter did not say clearly. What are the changes in the condition after recuperation? We know nothing about it. We can't wait to rush to the sickbed to comfort you! All we can do is quickly write letters, one letter, two letters, three letters, but the reply is always silent! Until today, whether you are alive or dead? We still can't understand! A weak body, how can it withstand the fierce attacks of vicious disease demons? No one could have expected that leaving in such a hurry without saying goodbye would indeed become a permanent farewell? More than ten months of heart-to-heart friendship has left us with endless pain! In the vast world, how many can be considered confidants? If you are dead, can death forget us? If you are dead, can you rest in peace? Aren't there still an old mother and young siblings in your family? Isn't there still a young wife whom you have been married to for a short time and shared the joys and sorrows with? Isn't there still a - no, he died long after he fell to the ground. The future is long, how will they live? If you are dead, can you close your eyes? Alas! God! Isn't this too painful!

But we still foolishly hope that your death will not become a reality, and we pray that there will be a day when we can meet you again!

XX! May you live healthily in the world!

He is now willing to work as a clerk in a foreign firm, company, or factory, or as a teacher in a family school. The salary is negotiable, and he has a reliable guarantor. If you are interested, please send a letter to Mr. Wang, c/o Zhonghongqiao Hongkou Elementary School.

He has a reliable guarantor and is negotiable on salary. Novel

Tomorrow (2) 272

— Mu Lin

He is my eldest sister's husband. I don't understand why I should think about him. That child also understands women's hearts too well. I think my eldest sister is very happy. Thinking, a black shadow rushed from the waist door again. Looking closely, it was my eldest sister. She was wearing a thin silk shirt, and her belly was slightly high in front. I wanted to laugh, but I couldn't laugh, as if I had done something hypocritical to her. I gently called out to my eldest sister, so low that it only rolled in my throat. My eldest sister sat beside me, stroking my arm and asked, "Are you sick?" I nodded, pretending to stand up reluctantly, and said, "The weather is not right. Mom is in the back." Then I took her hand and walked inside. My eldest sister kept calling out "Auntie" along the way. My mother came out of the kitchen with water dripping from her hands.

My eldest sister joked, "Auntie, my little sister is thinking of her brother-in-law. Look, her face is as red as a monkey's butt." I couldn't help but start to hit my elder sister, trying to tear her mouth. My mother came over to stop me and said, "Don't fight. Your elder sister is pregnant. If your brother-in-law finds out, he won't like it." Then I laughed, as if that lovely person was already standing in front of me.

After sitting down, my eldest sister said seriously, "Brother-in-law invites you to go to the movies." I glanced at my mother. She didn't seem to have heard [missing word] clearly, so I deliberately said that I wasn't comfortable today and didn't want to go. My eldest sister pursed her lips, "Is the little girl afraid of being seen by others?" I wanted to start hitting her again, but my mother said, "Your brother-in-law is kindly inviting you. Go ahead." It was clear that my mother had agreed. I still pretended to ask if my eldest sister was going. She pulled me and said as we walked, "Are you afraid your brother-in-law will eat you?"

When we arrived at my uncle and aunt's house, he was pacing back and forth in the hall. Today, he was wearing a new suit. The way his trouser legs swayed as he walked was quite stylish. When he saw us come in, his gaze shot at me, as if asking my eldest sister, "Is my sister going?" "My sister is afraid you'll eat her," my eldest sister's answer made everyone in the hall laugh.

After the movie, we ate dinner at a restaurant and returned to my uncle and aunt's house together. My eldest sister still escorted me back to my room. Whether it was on the tram, in the movie theater, or in the dining room, he was always carefully guarding against my eldest sister and me. He was guarding against my eldest sister, his wife. I felt that he had ulterior motives for being so attentive to me, because his eyes were always staring at me intensely after every move. Or maybe I'm just being too sensitive, but I hope my eldest sister doesn't notice these things.

Again, I have written so much. My mother often asks me what I am writing. Should I tell her? I have really changed recently.

Home
